add_namespace = hungary_flavor_eng


################
#UNITED KINGDOM#
################

# Hungary seeks entry into the Allies
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_eng.1
	title = hungary_flavor_eng.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_eng.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.34 }
		}
	}

	#Decline
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.35 }
		}
	}
}

# Danubian Conference arbitrated by Hungary
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_eng.2
	title = hungary_flavor_eng.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_eng.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_danube

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Let us hope for the best.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_danubian_coalition_may_join_the_allies
	}
}


# Hungary wants to switch sides
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_eng.3
	title = hungary_flavor_eng.3.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_eng.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_capitulation

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		HUN = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_ferenc_szalasi_is_ruler } }
	}

	#We'll support their attempts
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_government = neutrality }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				FROM = { has_government = democratic }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_eng.3.tt
		white_peace = FROM
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			white_peace = FROM
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "HUN"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.82 }
		}
	}

	#They will be liberated by force
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.84 }
		}
	}
}


# [From.GetName] asks for peace
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_eng.4
	title = hungary_flavor_eng.4.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_eng.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_capitulation

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Fair enough. We have other things to worry about.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		white_peace = FROM
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = ignore
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			white_peace = FROM
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = ignore
				id = "HUN"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { any_owned_state = { NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_claimed_by_HUN } } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_all_non_claimed_territory
			hidden_effect = { get_all_non_claimed_territory_from_hungary = yes }
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.121 }
		}
	}

	#We will not let them get away with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.122 }
		}
	}
}


# [From.GetName] offers their help against Romania
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_eng.5
	title = hungary_flavor_eng.5.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_eng.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We can use all the help we can get.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 83 } } add_state_claim = 83 }            #Grisana
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 84 } } add_state_claim = 84 }            #Transylvania
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 76 } } add_state_claim = 76 }            #North Transylvania
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 819 } } add_state_claim = 819 }        #Szeklerland
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 806 } } add_state_claim = 806 }        #Maramaros
			if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 807 } } add_state_claim = 807 }        #Northern Partium
			declare_war_on = { target = ROM type = puppet_wargoal_focus }
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
	}

	#We won't make deals with the devil.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_eng.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = {
					is_ahu = yes
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.128 }
		}
	}
}

#########
#FINLAND#
#########

# [From.GetAdjective] Alliance (event for Finland upon faction invite)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fin.1
	title = hungary_flavor_fin.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fin.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We need their help.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fin.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_defensive_war_with = SOV
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_invited_to_faction }
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.118 }
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
	}

	#We can hold our own just fine.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fin.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.119 }
		}
	}
}

# Hungary seeks membership in the Axis
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.1
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Welcome our Hungarian friends
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.1.a
		add_to_faction = FROM
		FROM = { country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.30 } }
	}

	#We are better off without them
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.1.b
		FROM = { country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.31 } }
	}
}

# Communism victorious
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.2
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = GER
		has_government = communism
		has_idea = communist_revolution
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	#Internationalism is the way to go.
	option = {
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_government = communism
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.2.a
		remove_ideas = communist_revolution
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor_ger.3 }
		}
	}

	#We need to continue the revolution on our own.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.2.b
		remove_ideas = communist_revolution
	}
}

		}

# Assisting Hungary
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.9
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.9.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_inspect_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We can spare a few generals
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.9.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		remove_unit_leader = 13
		remove_unit_leader = 17
		effect_tooltip = { HUN = { add_ideas = { assistance_from_german_general_staff } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_germany_full_help
				country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.94 }
			}
		}
	}

	#Send a token mission of military advisors
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		effect_tooltip = { HUN = { add_ideas = { assistance_from_german_general_staff } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_germany_partial_help
				country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.94 }
			}
		}
	}

	#They do not have our support
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_germany_no_help
				country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.95 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Overlord of Austria asked about Anschluss
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.11
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.11.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Accept
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				GER = { has_army_size = { size < 40 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				GER = { has_army_size = { size > 39 } }
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { hours = 2 id = germany.4 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Refuse
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = { has_army_size = { size > 39 } }
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				GER = { has_army_size = { size < 30 } }
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = GER_anschluss_rejected }
			country_event = { hours = 2 id = germany.29 }
			if = { limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Fate of Czechoslovakia event for the overlord of CZE
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.12
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.12.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Agree
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_puppet = yes
					GER = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
					GER = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = SOV
							OR = {
								has_war_with = ENG
								has_war_with = FRA
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						any_country = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					}
					GER = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_war_with = ENG
								NOT = {
									has_war_with = FRA
								}
							}
							AND = {
								has_war_with = FRA
								NOT = {
									has_war_with = ENG
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = germany.55 }
	}
	option = { # Refuse
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
				NOT = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					any_country = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				}
				is_puppet = no
				NOT = {
					GER = {
						has_war_with = ENG
						has_war_with = FRA
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					GER = {
						has_war_with = SOV
						OR = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				GER = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_war_with = ENG
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = FRA
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_war_with = FRA
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ENG
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = germany.54 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Meeting with Horthy
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.14

		text = hungary_flavor_ger.14.d_nothing
		trigger = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_nothing }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_ger.14.d_carpathian_ruthenia
		trigger = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_carpathian_ruthenia }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_ger.14.d_slovakia
		trigger = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_slovakia }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_hitler_horthy_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We can agree to these requests.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.14.a

			NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_nothing }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.116 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_carpathian_ruthenia }
				set_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_slovakia }
				set_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia
			}
		}
	}

	#We can make no promises.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.14.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_nothing }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.117 } }
	}

	#We will be carving up Czechoslovakia on our own terms then.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.14.c
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_wants_nothing
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing }
	}
}

# The Fate of Czechoslovakia (fixing inexplicable conflict with vanilla files)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.15
	title = germany.53.t
	desc = {
		text = germany.55.d
		trigger = { has_global_flag = end_of_czechoslovakia }
	}
	desc = {
		text = germany.55.d_2
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = end_of_czechoslovakia } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_inspect_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex CZE, puppet SLO, ignore Carpathian Ruthenia
	option = {
		name = germany.55.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			SLO = { exists = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				70 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			SLO = { transfer_state = 70 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				71 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			SLO = { transfer_state = 71 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				818 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			SLO = { transfer_state = 818 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				73 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			RUT = { transfer_state = 73 }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				802 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			RUT = { transfer_state = 802 }    #Berehovo
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing }
				country_exists = HUN
				802 = { is_owned_by = HUN }
			}
			HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.104 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia }
			HUN = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_betrayed_promises } }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				664 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			SLO = { transfer_state = 664 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CZE }
			annex_country = { target = CZE }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SLO = { NOT = { is_subject = yes } } }    #If Slovakia is already a puppet, GER doesn't steal it
			puppet = SLO
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				72 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
				country_exists = POL
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = 72 } # Give Poland Zaolzie
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				72 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = POL }
			}
			SLO = { transfer_state = 72 } # Give Slovakia Zaolzie
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { hours = 6 id = news.60 }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = SLO
				}
				add_core_of = SLO
			}
			SLO = {
				load_oob = SLO_1939
				add_manpower = 9876
			}
		}
	}
	#Annex CZE, give Hungary SLO and Carpathian Ruthenia
	option = {
		name = germany.55.b
		add_political_power = -20
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing
					AND = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia }
						NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing }
						NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia }
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			664 = { is_owned_by = HUN }
			HUN = {
				is_friend_or_potential_friend_of_GER = yes
			}
		}
		HUN = { country_event = germany.56 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				72 = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = CZE
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = 72 } # Give Poland Zaolzie
		}
	}
	#Annex everything
	option = {
		name = germany.55.c
		add_political_power = -50
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					SLO = { exists = no }    #If Slovakia exists, the first option is disabled, which leaves us with this one
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia
						has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia }
							NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_nothing }
							NOT = { has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia }
							is_historical_focus_on = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_carpathian_ruthenia
					has_global_flag = HUN_GER_agreement_hungary_gets_slovakia
				}
			}
			HUN = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_betrayed_promises } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CZE }
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUT = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = CZE
					}
				}
				annex_country = { target = RUT }
			}
			annex_country = { target = CZE }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { hours = 6 id = news.62 }
		}
	}
}

# The Kaiser's Coup
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.22
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.22.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_cavalry

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# The country will stand fast against this insurgence.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.22.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_royalist_supporters_will_start_a_civil_war
		set_global_flag = HUN_kaisers_coup_started
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.1 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.1
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.1
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.2 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.2
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.2
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.3 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.3
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.3
				}
			}
			if = {

					NOT = { neutrality > 0.4 }

				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.4
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.4
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.5 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.5
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.5
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.6 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.6
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.6
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.6
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.7 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.7
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.7
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.7
					NOT = { neutrality > 0.8 }
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.8
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.8
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality > 0.8
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.9
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					set_equipment_fraction = 0.9
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = GER
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = GER_IMP
			}
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_promised_some_equipment_to_royalist_germany } }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					if = {
						limit = { HUN = { has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons } }
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 10000 producer = HUN }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { HUN = { has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons } }
								add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 10000 producer = HUN }
								else = {
									add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 10000 producer = HUN }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { HUN = { has_tech = artillery4 } }
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_3 amount = 1000 producer = HUN }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { HUN = { has_tech = artillery1 } }
								add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_2 amount = 1000 producer = HUN }
								else = {
									add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 1000 producer = HUN }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = 2000 producer = HUN }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = motorized_equipment_1 amount = 3000 producer = HUN }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_promised_lots_of_equipment_to_royalist_germany } }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					if = {
						limit = { HUN = { has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons } }
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 20000 producer = HUN }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { HUN = { has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons } }
								add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 20000 producer = HUN }
								else = {
									add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 20000 producer = HUN }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { HUN = { has_tech = artillery4 } }
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_3 amount = 2000 producer = HUN }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { HUN = { has_tech = artillery1 } }
								add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_2 amount = 2000 producer = HUN }
								else = {
									add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 2000 producer = HUN }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = 4000 producer = HUN }
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = motorized_equipment_1 amount = 6000 producer = HUN }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_promised_to_fight_for_royalist_germany } }
				HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.160 } }
			}
			HUN = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = stockpiling_equipment_25 }
					remove_ideas = stockpiling_equipment_25
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = stockpiling_equipment_50 }
					remove_ideas = stockpiling_equipment_50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Kaiser's Coup succeeds
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ger.23
	title = hungary_flavor_ger.23.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ger.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_royal_parade

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		original_tag = GER
		has_global_flag = HUN_kaisers_coup_started
		has_government = neutrality
		all_country = {
			OR = {
				tag = ROOT
				NOT = { original_tag = GER }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	# Long live the new German Empire!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ger.23.a
		hidden_effect = {
			HUN = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = secret_agents_occupied }
					remove_ideas = secret_agents_occupied
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = hun_news.13 }
		}
		add_ideas = german_empire_reborn
	}
}

# Hidden events of the Hungarian Flavor mod #

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_hidden

# These events are hidden, so they do not need to be localised, they don't need titles, descriptions, or pictures

# Removing "Receiving Supplies from Slovakia", if Slovakia doesn't exist anymore, or isn't a Hungarian subject
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_hidden.1

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		has_idea = receiving_supplies_from_slovakia
		SLO = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				NOT = { is_subject_of = HUN }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_hidden.1.a
		remove_ideas = receiving_supplies_from_slovakia
	}
}

# Removing "Sending Supplies to Hungary" from Slovakia, if Slovakia isn't a Hungarian subject

		date < 1949.1.1

		has_idea = sending_supplies_to_hungary
		NOT = { is_subject_of = HUN }
	}

		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_hidden.2.a
		remove_ideas = sending_supplies_to_hungary
	}
}

# Reassigning Trianon backer status, in case the previous one got annexed
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_hidden.6

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		all_country = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_policing_expansion_of_hungary }
		}
		any_country = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_backed_out_from_treaty_of_trianon }
			is_major = yes
			OR = {
				tag = ENG
				tag = FRA
				tag = USA
				tag = ENG
				tag = ITA
				tag = JAP
				tag = BEL
				tag = CHI
				tag = CUB
				tag = GRE
				tag = NIC
				tag = PAN
				tag = POL
				tag = POR
				tag = ROM
				tag = YUG
				tag = SIA
				tag = CZE
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_hidden.6.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				ENG = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_backed_out_from_treaty_of_trianon }
				}
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.34 days = 1 } }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FRA = {
							exists = yes
							NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_backed_out_from_treaty_of_trianon }
						}
					}
					FRA = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.34 days = 1 } }
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								USA = {
									exists = yes
									NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_backed_out_from_treaty_of_trianon }
								}
							}
							USA = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.34 days = 1 } }
							else = {
								random_country = {
									limit = {
										is_major = yes
										NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_backed_out_from_treaty_of_trianon }
										OR = {
											# These are the rest of the countries who signed the treaty in 1920
											tag = ITA
											tag = JAP
											tag = BEL
											tag = CHI
											tag = CUB
											tag = GRE
											tag = NIC
											tag = PAN
											tag = POL
											tag = POR
											tag = ROM
											tag = YUG
											tag = SIA
											tag = CZE
										}
									}
									country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.34 days = 1 }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#############################
# Horthy inheritance events #
#############################

# Events related to the inheritance of Horthy's regent position
# These are only relevant, if Horthy has maintained his regency, without electing a king, or abolishing the monarchy

add_namespace = horthy_inheritance

# Istvn Horthy dies in plane crash
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.10
	title = horthy_inheritance.10.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_istvan_horthy_death

	trigger = {
		tag = HUN
		date > 1933.1.1
		date > 1939.1.1
		has_war = yes
		#has_deployed_air_force_size > 1	# To check whether the country is using the air force at all
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_decomissioned }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead }
		has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead
	}

	# The nation mourns with the Horthy family.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.10.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { hours = 8 id = horthy_inheritance.12 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { hours = 8 id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
				clr_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { date > 1941.1.17 }
			set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_available    # Istvn's son was born on January 17th 1941
		}
	}
}

# Istvn Horthy survives plane crash
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.11
	title = horthy_inheritance.11.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_istvan_horthy_survives

	trigger = {
		tag = HUN
		date > 1939.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_war = yes
		#has_deployed_air_force_size > 1	# To check whether the country is using the air force at all
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_decomissioned }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead }
		has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_decomissioned
	}

	# Get him home before anything worse happens.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.11.a
	}
}

# The question of Horthy's inheritance
# (After Istvn Horthy's plane crash)
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.12
	title = horthy_inheritance.12.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# A successor will be chosen
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.12.a
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
	}

	# There is no need to worry about that yet
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.12.b
		add_political_power = -5
	}
}

# Horthy's health declines
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.20
	title = horthy_inheritance.20.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	trigger = {
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 96
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1941.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1942.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1943.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1944.1.1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_horthy_bad_health1
	}

	# A successor will be chosen
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.20.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
		}
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
	}

	# There is no need to worry about that yet
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.20.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}

	# Good thing the succession is secured
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.20.c
		trigger = {
			horthy_inheritance_settled = yes
		}
	}
}

# Horthy's health declines further
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.21
	title = horthy_inheritance.21.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_bad_health1
		has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1942.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1943.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1944.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1945.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1946.1.1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_horthy_bad_health2
	}

	# A successor will be chosen
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.21.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
		}
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
	}

	# There is no need to worry about that yet
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.21.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
		}
		add_political_power = -20
	}

	# Good thing the succession is secured
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.21.c
		trigger = {
			horthy_inheritance_settled = yes
		}
	}
}

# Horthy dies
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.22
	title = horthy_inheritance.22.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1933.1.1
				date < 1957.2.1
				has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_bad_health2
				has_country_leader = { character = HUN_miklos_horthy ruling_only = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1957.2.7
				date < 1957.2.8
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1944.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1945.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1946.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1947.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			date > 1948.1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0000000001
			date < 1957.2.1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_horthy_dead
	}

	# We cannot delay this decision further. We have to choose a successor.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.22.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { horthy_inheritance_settled = yes }
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		kill_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reinstate_horthy }
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_as_chief_of_navy } }
			remove_ideas = horthy
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 110
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.101 }
	}

	# Let the successor assume his rightful position
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.22.b
		trigger = {
			horthy_inheritance_settled = yes
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_reinstate_horthy }
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_as_chief_of_navy } }
			remove_ideas = horthy
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 110
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.102 }
	}
}

# Horthy retires
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.23
	title = horthy_inheritance.23.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# He has served the country well. It is time for his successor to take over.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.23.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor }
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
					create_politician_king_istvan_horthy = yes
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
						remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
					}
					set_country_flag = HUN_has_king
					else = { create_politician_istvan_horthy = yes }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_successor }
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
					create_politician_king_istvan_horthy_jr = yes
					else = { create_politician_istvan_horthy_jr = yes }
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
						remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
					}
					set_country_flag = HUN_has_king
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_successor }
				create_politician_victor_emmanuel = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
					remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
				}
				set_country_flag = HUN_has_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_wilhelm_hohenzollern_successor }
				create_politician_wilhelm_hohenzollern_hun = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
					remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
				}
				set_country_flag = HUN_has_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_otto_habsburg_successor }
				promote_character = HUN_otto_von_habsburg
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
					remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
				}
				set_country_flag = HUN_has_king
				news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Choosing Horthy's successor
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.100
	title = horthy_inheritance.100.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Horthy's son, Istvn Horthy
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.100.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead }
		}
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_will_succeed_to_regency
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_will_succeed_to_throne
			}
		}
	}

	# Horthy's grandson, Istvn Horthy jr.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.100.b
		#trigger = {
		#	has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead
		#	has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_available
		#}
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_will_succeed_to_regency
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_will_succeed_to_throne
			}
		}
	}

	# The Italian king, Victor Emmanuel
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.100.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_forbidden_from_claiming_throne }
			ITA = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_victor_emmanuel_will_succeed_to_throne
		ITA = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ita.8 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
		}
	}

	# The German crown prince, Wilhelm
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.100.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_wilhelm_von_hohenzollern_forbidden_from_claiming_throne }
			GER = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_wilhelm_von_hohenzollern_will_succeed_to_throne
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ger.20 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
		}
	}

	# The head of the Habsburg dynasty, Otto
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.100.f
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_otto_habsburg_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_otto_von_habsburg_will_succeed_to_throne
	}
}

# Electing Mikls Horthy's successor
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.101
	title = horthy_inheritance.101.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_horthy_inheritance

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Horthy's son, Istvn Horthy
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.101.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead }
		}
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_will_succeed_to_regency
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.102 } }
	}

	# Horthy's grandson, Istvn Horthy jr.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.101.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_dead
			has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_available
		}
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_will_succeed_to_regency
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.102 } }
	}

	# The Italian king, Victor Emmanuel

		name = horthy_inheritance.101.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_forbidden_from_claiming_throne }
			ITA = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_victor_emmanuel_will_succeed_to_throne
		ITA = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ita.8 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
		}
	}

	# The German crown prince, Wilhelm
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.101.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_wilhelm_von_hohenzollern_forbidden_from_claiming_throne }
			GER = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_upon_the_death_of_horthy
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_wilhelm_von_hohenzollern_will_succeed_to_throne
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ger.20 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
		}
	}

	# The head of the Habsburg dynasty, Otto
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.101.f
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_otto_habsburg_successor
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_otto_von_habsburg_will_succeed_to_throne
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.102 } }
	}
}

# The new head of state
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.102
	title = horthy_inheritance.102.t
	desc = {
		text = horthy_inheritance.102.d_istvan
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor }
	}
	desc = {
		text = horthy_inheritance.102.d_istvan_jr
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_successor }
	}
	desc = {
		text = horthy_inheritance.102.d_victor
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_successor }
	}
	desc = {
		text = horthy_inheritance.102.d_wilhelm
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_wilhelm_hohenzollern_successor }
	}
	desc = {
		text = horthy_inheritance.102.d_otto
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_otto_habsburg_successor }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_royal_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Long may he reign!
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.102.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_successor }
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
					create_politician_king_istvan_horthy = yes
					else = { create_politician_istvan_horthy = yes }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_istvan_horthy_jr_successor }
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = HUN_enthrone_horthy }
					create_politician_king_istvan_horthy_jr = yes
					else = { create_politician_istvan_horthy_jr = yes }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_successor }
				create_politician_victor_emmanuel = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_wilhelm_hohenzollern_successor }
				create_politician_wilhelm_hohenzollern_hun = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_otto_habsburg_successor }
				promote_character = HUN_otto_von_habsburg
				news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Victor Emmanuel accepts the crown
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.110
	title = horthy_inheritance.110.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.110.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We will make the necessary arrangements.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.110.a
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_successor
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_dead }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.102 } }
		}
	}
}

# Victor Emmanuel unable to accept the Hungarian crown
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.111
	title = horthy_inheritance.111.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.111.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Let us review our options then.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.111.a
		set_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_forbidden_from_claiming_throne
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_horthy_dead }
			country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.101 }
			else = {
				country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Victor Emmanuel no longer eligible for the Hungarian throne
country_event = {
	id = horthy_inheritance.112
	title = horthy_inheritance.112.t
	desc = horthy_inheritance.112.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_successor
		has_war_with = ITA
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	# We will choose someone else then.
	option = {
		name = horthy_inheritance.112.a
		clear_horthy_inheritance = yes
		set_country_flag = HUN_victor_emmanuel_forbidden_from_claiming_throne
		country_event = { id = horthy_inheritance.100 }
	}
}

add_namespace = hungary_flavor

#HUNGARY#

# Welcome to Hungarian Flavor
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.1
	title = hungary_flavor.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	#Realism
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor.1.realism
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.3 } }
	}

	#No realism
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor.1.no_realism
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = HUN_realism }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.3 } }
	}
}

# Union with Austria
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.2
	title = hungary_flavor.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor.2.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			#load_oob = AUS_troops_replace
			set_cosmetic_tag = AUH
			every_state = { if = { limit = { is_core_of = AUS } add_core_of = HUN } }        #transfering cores
			every_state = { if = { limit = { is_claimed_by = AUS } add_claim_by = HUN } }    #transfering claims
			upgrade_multinationality = yes
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 0
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 100
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = HUN_federationists name = HUN_federationists }
			set_party_name = { ideology = communism long_name = HUN_komp_long name = HUN_komp }
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = HUN_imperialists name = HUN_imperialists }
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = HUN_AHU_supremacists_long name = HUN_AHU_supremacists }

			create_politician_otto_von_habsburg_ahu = yes
			set_country_flag = HUN_has_king

			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = kingdom_without_a_king }
				remove_ideas = kingdom_without_a_king
			}

			AUS = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = HUN
				}
			}
			create_military_joseph_von_habsburg = yes
			annex_country = { target = AUS transfer_troops = yes }
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.29 }

			#ROOT has been a badboy
			add_to_variable = { var = global.HUN_badboy_rating value = 1 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
					has_country_flag = HUN_policing_expansion_of_hungary
				}
				hidden_effect = { worsen_relations_with_HUN = yes }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_their_opinion_of_us_will_deteriorate
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.4 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Romania issues a counterdemand!
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.20
	title = hungary_flavor.20.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_alfold_to_romania

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		ROM = { add_state_claim = 154 }    #Alfld
	}

	#This means war.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = { target = ROM type = annex_everything }
		ROM = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_rom.6 } }
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}

	#What a preposterous idea.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
				create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
			type = take_state_focus
			target = ROM
			generator = { 810 76 810 84 83 45 }
		}
		ROM = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_rom.6 } }
	}

	#We didn't expect this. Withdraw from the Transtisza region.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.20.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				transfer_state = 154 #Alfld
				if = {
					limit = { HUN = { owns_state = 45 } }    #Torontal
					transfer_state = 45 #Torontal
				}
			}
			country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_rom.7 }
		}
	}
}

# Italian Negotiations
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.23
	title = hungary_flavor.23.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Propose a non-aggression pact
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.23.a
		ITA = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_ita.2 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_if_italy_accepts_colon
		effect_tooltip = { diplomatic_relation = { country = ITA relation = non_aggression_pact } }
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_non_aggression_pact }
	}

	#Offer military support
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ITA = { owns_state = 801 }    #Fiume
				ITA = { owns_state = 163 }    #Zara
				ITA = { owns_state = 736 }    #Istria
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor.23.b
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.24 }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 163 } }    #Zara
					country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.25 }
					else = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.26 } }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_be_able_to_request_territory_in_return
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_if_italy_accepts_colon
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_transfer_some_equipment_to_italy
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_non_aggression_pact }
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_military_support }
	}

	#Offer military and political support
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.23.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ITA = { owns_state = 801 }    #Fiume
				ITA = { owns_state = 163 }    #Zara
				ITA = { owns_state = 736 }    #Istria
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.24 }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 163 } }    #Zara
					country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.25 }
					else = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.26 } }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_be_able_to_request_territory_in_return
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_if_italy_accepts_colon
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_transfer_some_equipment_to_italy
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_back_italian_territorial_expansion
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_non_aggression_pact }
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_military_support }
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_political_support }
	}
}

# The question of Fiume
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.24
	title = hungary_flavor.24.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We will include Fiume in the proposal
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.24.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_if_italy_accepts_colon
		effect_tooltip = { transfer_state = 801 }    #Fiume
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_fiume_plus }
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 163 } }    #Zara
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.25 }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 736 } }    #Istria
					country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.26 }
					else = { ITA = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_ita.2 } } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#We do not need Fiume
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.24.b
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 163 } }    #Zara
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.25 }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { ITA = { owns_state = 736 } }    #Istria
					country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.26 }
					else = { ITA = { country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_ita.2 } } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Italy accepts_conditions
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.27
	title = hungary_flavor.27.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#A successful agreement.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.27.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_italian_treaty }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_italian_treaty }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_non_aggression_pact }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = ITA relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_military_support }
			send_equipment = { target = ITA type = infantry_equipment amount = 10000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_political_support }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = supporting_italy days = 548 }
			ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = support_from_hungary days = 548 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_fiume_plus }
			transfer_state = 801    #Fiume
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_zara_plus }
			transfer_state = 163    #Zara
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_istria_plus }
			transfer_state = 736    #Istria
		}
	}
}

# The Danubian Conference
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.36
	title = hungary_flavor.36.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_danube

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Let the event commence.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.36.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = HUN
					tag = GRE
					tag = BUL
					tag = ALB

				set_nationality = HUN
			}
		}
		annex_country = { target = CZE transfer_troops = yes }
		add_war_support = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			#ROOT has been a badboy
			add_to_variable = { var = global.HUN_badboy_rating value = 1 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
					has_country_flag = HUN_policing_expansion_of_hungary
				}
				hidden_effect = { worsen_relations_with_HUN = yes }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_their_opinion_of_us_will_deteriorate
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.4 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
		news_event = { hours = 2 id = hun_news.32 }
	}
}

				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria }

					805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana

					news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		868 = { NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden } }    #Murakz

# Alliance with Yugoslavia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.60
	title = hungary_flavor.60.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.60.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		is_faction_leader = yes
		has_country_flag = HUN_YUG_eternal_friendship
		YUG = {
			exists = yes
			is_puppet = no
			is_in_faction = no
			has_opinion = { target = ROOT value > 49 }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_government = fascism
				YUG = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			AND = {
				has_government = communism
				YUG = { has_government = communism }
			}
			AND = {
				has_government = democratic
				YUG = { has_government = democratic }
			}
			YUG = { has_government = neutrality }
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 183 }

	#Of course, we shall invite them.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.60.a
		YUG = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_yug.3 } }
	}

		name = hungary_flavor.60.b
	}
}

					has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHU
					has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHF
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_retain_current_map_color
		}
	}

	#Vienna it is.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.67.b
		set_capital = {
			state = 4
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHU }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_change_map_color_to_white
			hidden_effect = { set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHU_WHITE }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHF }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_change_map_color_to_white
			hidden_effect = { set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHF_WHITE }
		}
	}
}

# Possible exit attempt
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.78
	title = hungary_flavor.78.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.78.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_capitulation

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		is_in_faction_with = GER
		surrender_progress > 0.2
		OR = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			ENG = {
				exists = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	#We will consider our options
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.78.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_exit_attempt
	}

	#We will be forever loyal to the Axis
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.78.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

	desc = hungary_flavor.85.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = hungary_flavor.85.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor.85.tt
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			GER = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
					freedom_level = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 100
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 0
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}

	#Get ready to fight!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.85.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		GER = {
			remove_from_faction = ROOT
		}
		start_civil_war = { ideology = fascism size = 0.5 }
	}
}

# Trianon restrictions invalidated
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.98
	title = hungary_flavor.98.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.98.d
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.98.d_2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				threat > 0.50
				date > 1940.1.1
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_trianon

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		has_idea = trianon_restrictions
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			OR = {
				threat > 0.50
				date > 1940.1.1
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	#Together we are strong.
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
		}
		name = hungary_flavor.98.a
		remove_ideas = trianon_restrictions
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_secret_rearmament }
			remove_ideas = HUN_secret_rearmament
		}
	}

	#Were those restrictions still valid? I didn't notice.
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				threat > 0.50
				date > 1940.1.1
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor.98.b
		remove_ideas = trianon_restrictions
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_secret_rearmament }
			remove_ideas = HUN_secret_rearmament
		}
	}
}

# Gyri Program goes against Trianon restrictions
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.99
	title = hungary_flavor.99.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.99.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_trianon

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We will openly disobey the constraints
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.99.a
		add_political_power = -100
		remove_ideas = trianon_restrictions
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = HUN_secret_rearmament }
			remove_ideas = HUN_secret_rearmament
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_policing_expansion_of_hungary
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = PREV
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_disobeyed_trianon_restrictions }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = HUN_gyori_program }
	}

	#Perform the restricted research in secret
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.99.b
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = HUN_gyori_program }
	}

	#Try our best to stay within the boundaries.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.99.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor.99.tt
		#hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = HUN_gyori_program_hindered }
		multiply_variable = { var = global.HUN_gyori_program_phase_duration value = 1.2 }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = HUN_gyori_program }
	}
}


# The Visegrd Group (founding)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.100
	title = hungary_flavor.100.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.100.d_both
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.100.d_cze
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.100.d_pol
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.100.d_neither
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_visegrad_group

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#The Visegrd Triangle is strong.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.100.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus
		}
		set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
		create_faction = visegrad_group_faction
		add_to_faction = POL
		add_to_faction = CZE
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
			CZE = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			POL = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "POL"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "CZE"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "HUN"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.4 }
	}

	#We will build a strong alliance with Czechoslovakia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.100.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
		set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
		create_faction = visegrad_group_faction
		add_to_faction = CZE
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "CZE"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "HUN"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.4 }
	}

	#At least our Polish friends are willing to join
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.100.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
		set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
		create_faction = visegrad_group_faction
		add_to_faction = POL
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "POL"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "HUN"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.4 }
	}

	#It seems this alliance died before it could be born
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.100.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus
		}
	}
}

			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.101.d_none
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus
			has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_visegrad_group

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Let us welcome the new members.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.101.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = LIT
		add_to_faction = LAT
		add_to_faction = EST
		LIT = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
		LAT = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
		EST = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = LAT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = LAT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = EST modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = EST modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_technology_circle_present }
			LIT = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			LAT = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			EST = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_military_council_present }
			LIT = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
			LAT = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
			EST = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "LAT"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "LIT"
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "EST"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Let us welcome the new members.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.101.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus }
			add_to_faction = LIT
			LIT = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = LIT }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = LIT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_technology_circle_present }
				LIT = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_military_council_present }
				LIT = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = LIT }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = "LIT"
						value = 200
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus }
			add_to_faction = LAT
			LAT = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = LAT }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = LAT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = LAT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_technology_circle_present }
				LAT = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_military_council_present }
				LAT = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = LAT }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = "LAT"
						value = 200
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
			add_to_faction = EST
			EST = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = EST }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = EST modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = EST modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_technology_circle_present }
				EST = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_military_council_present }
				EST = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = EST }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = "EST"
						value = 200
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#A disappointing result.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.101.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus
			}
		}
	}
}

# Federalisation of Austria-Hungary
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.102
	title = hungary_flavor.102.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.102.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_renounced_claims_towards_poland }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor.102.d_no_galicia
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_renounced_claims_towards_poland
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_wilsons_10th

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			create_politician_otto_von_habsburg_ahu = yes
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = HUN_conservatives name = HUN_conservatives }
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = HUN_federationists name = HUN_federationists }
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 0
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 100
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#It shall be called the Austro-Hungarian Federation
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.102.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_federationists_will_become_the_ruling_party
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHF
	}

	#It shall be called the Danubian Federation
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.102.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_federationists_will_become_the_ruling_party
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_DNF
	}

	#Let's call it the United States of Greater Hungary
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.102.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_federationists_will_become_the_ruling_party
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_USH
	}
}

# Hungarian-Slovakian Small War
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.106
	title = hungary_flavor.106.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.106.d
	picture = GFX_hun_slo_small_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		has_country_flag = HUN_first_vienna_award
		OR = {
			owns_state = 73 # Carpathian Ruthenia
			RUT = {
				owns_state = 73        # Carpathian Ruthenia
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		OR = {
			SLO = {
				exists = yes
				owns_state = 818 #Sobrance
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			CZE = {
				exists = yes
				owns_state = 818 #Sobrance
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	#A great success for out nation.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.106.a
		add_manpower = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { SLO = { exists = yes } } SLO = { country_event = { hours = 1 id = hungary_flavor_cze.7 } } }
			if = { limit = { CZE = { exists = yes } } CZE = { country_event = { hours = 1 id = hungary_flavor_cze.7 } } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 73 }        # Carpathian Ruthenia
			transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUT = { owns_state = 73 } }        # Carpathian Ruthenia
			RUT = { transfer_state = 818 }    #Sobrance
		}
	}
}

# Peace with Britain

	id = hungary_flavor.120
	title = hungary_flavor.120.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.120.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_degaulle_churchill

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_war_with = ENG
		ENG = { has_country_flag = decree_against_hungary }
	}

	#Send the offer.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.120.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		ENG = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_eng.4 }
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_state = { NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_claimed_by_HUN } } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_all_non_claimed_territory
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_britain_and_allies_will_peace_out
				custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
			}
		}
	}

	#We are not done with this war yet.
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = hungary_flavor.120.b
	}
}
