# Slovakian self governance
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.123
	title = hungary_flavor.123.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.123.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	is_triggered_only = yes    #From decision

	#We will not set up a new government.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.123.a
	}

	#Set up all of Slovakia as a puppet state.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.123.b
		SLO = {
			transfer_state = 70        #Western Slovakia
			add_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
			transfer_state = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			add_state_core = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
			add_state_core = 818    #Sobrance
			transfer_state = 664    #Southern Slovakia
			add_state_core = 664    #Southern Slovakia
		}
		if = { limit = { 70 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 70 }                #Western Slovakia
		70 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Western Slovakia
		if = { limit = { 71 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 71 }                #Eastern Slovakia
		71 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Eastern Slovakia
		if = { limit = { 818 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 818 }                #Sobrance
		818 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Sobrance
		if = { limit = { 664 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 664 }                #Southern Slovakia
		664 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Southern Slovakia
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SLO
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = SLO }
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.182 } }
	}

	#Set up Northern Slovakia as a puppet state.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.123.c
		SLO = {
			transfer_state = 70        #Western Slovakia
			add_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
			transfer_state = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			add_state_core = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
			add_state_core = 818    #Sobrance
		}
		if = { limit = { 70 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 70 }                #Western Slovakia
		70 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Western Slovakia
		if = { limit = { 71 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 71 }                #Eastern Slovakia
		71 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Eastern Slovakia
		if = { limit = { 818 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 818 }                #Sobrance
		818 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Sobrance
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SLO
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = SLO }
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.182 } }
	}
}

# The Second Hungarian Republic
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.126
	title = hungary_flavor.126.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.126.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_journalists_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Long live the republic!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.126.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			add_ideas = democracy_gaining_ground
			remove_ideas = conservative_ideas
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_current_cabinet_will_take_power
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { date < 1938.5.15 }
					create_politician_kalman_daranyi = yes
					set_country_flag = HUN_daranyi_president
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date > 1938.5.14
						date < 1939.2.17
					}
					create_politician_bela_imredy = yes
					set_country_flag = HUN_imredy_president
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = HUN_bela_imredy }
						remove_ideas = HUN_bela_imredy
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date > 1939.2.16
						date < 1941.4.4
					}
					create_politician_pal_teleki = yes
					set_country_flag = HUN_teleki_president
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						date > 1941.4.3
						date < 1942.3.8
					}
					create_politician_laszlo_bardossy = yes
					set_country_flag = HUN_bardossy_president
				}
				if = {
					limit = { date > 1942.3.7 }
					create_politician_miklos_kallay = yes
					set_country_flag = HUN_kallay_president
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = HUN_bela_imredy }
						remove_ideas = HUN_bela_imredy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = democratic }
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_cosmetic_tag = HUN_REP }
	}
}

# Austria joins the Visegrd Group
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.129
	title = hungary_flavor.129.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.129.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Let us welcome them.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.129.a
		add_to_faction = AUS
		AUS = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = AUS }
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUS modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_technology_circle_present }
			AUS = { add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_military_council_present }
			AUS = { add_ideas = visegrad_military_council }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = AUS }
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance

		}
	}

# Polish refugees
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.138
	title = hungary_flavor.138.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.138.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_polish_refugees

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_allowing_german_troops_through }
		OR = {
			owns_state = 70        #Western Slovakia
			owns_state = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			owns_state = 818    #Sobrance
			owns_state = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			is_neighbor_of = POL
		}
		POL = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
			exists = yes
			has_war_with = GER
			NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
			surrender_progress > 0.5
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 14
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	#Let them in.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.138.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_allowed_polish_refugees_through_pos }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_with = POL
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_allowed_polish_refugees_through_neg }
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = POL
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				hidden_effect = { add_manpower = 10000 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_receive_refugees
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ENG = {
							exists = yes
							OR = {
								is_in_faction_with = POL
								has_war_with = GER
							}
						}
					}
					ENG = {
						hidden_effect = { add_manpower = 10000 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_receive_refugees
					}
					else = {
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = POL
									has_war_with = GER
								}
							}
							hidden_effect = { add_manpower = 10000 }
							custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_receive_refugees
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#They have no place within our borders
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.138.b
	}
}

# Self governance of Carpathian Ruthenia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.144
	title = hungary_flavor.144.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.144.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes    #From decision

	#We will not set up a new government.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.144.a
	}

	#Set up all of Carpathian Ukraine as a puppet state.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.144.b
		RUT = {
			transfer_state = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			add_state_core = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			transfer_state = 802    #Beregszasz
			add_state_core = 802    #Beregszasz
		}
		if = { limit = { 73 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 73 }                #Carpathian Ruthenia
		73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		if = { limit = { 802 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 802 }                #Beregszasz
		802 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Beregszasz
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = RUT
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = RUT }
		}
	}

	#Keep Berehovo, they can have the rest.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.144.c
		RUT = {
			transfer_state = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			add_state_core = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = RUT
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = RUT }
		}
		if = { limit = { 73 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 73 }                #Carpathian Ruthenia
		73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
	}
}

# Joining Slovakia and Carpathian Ruthenia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.145
	title = hungary_flavor.145.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.145.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes    #From Decision

	#Slovakia will get all of Carpathian Ruthenia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.145.a
		SLO = {
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { NOT = { owns_state = 73 } } }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
				transfer_state = 73    #Carpathian Ruthenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { NOT = { owns_state = 818 } } }    #Sobrance
				transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { NOT = { owns_state = 802 } } }    #Berehovo
				transfer_state = 802    #Berehovo
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 73 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 73 }                #Carpathian Ruthenia
		73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		if = { limit = { 818 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 818 }                #Sobrance
		818 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Sobrance
		if = { limit = { 802 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 802 }                #Berehovo
		802 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Berehovo
	}

	#Slovakia will get the northern parts of Carpathian Ruthenia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.145.b
		SLO = {
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { NOT = { owns_state = 73 } } }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
				transfer_state = 73    #Carpathian Ruthenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SLO = { NOT = { owns_state = 818 } } }    #Sobrance
				transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 73 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 73 }                #Carpathian Ruthenia
		73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		if = { limit = { 818 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 818 }                #Sobrance
		818 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Sobrance
	}
}

# Transylvanian self governance
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.148
	title = hungary_flavor.148.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.148.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	is_triggered_only = yes    #From decision

	#We will not set up a new government.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.148.a
	}

	#Set up Transylvania as a puppet state.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.148.b
		TRA = {
			transfer_state = 76        #North Transylvania
			add_state_core = 76        #North Transylvania
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { owns_state = 819 } }    #Szeklerland
				transfer_state = 819    #Szeklerland
				add_state_core = 819    #Szeklerland
			}
			transfer_state = 82        #Banat
			add_state_core = 82        #Banat
			transfer_state = 83        #Southern Partium
			add_state_core = 83        #Southern Partium
			transfer_state = 84        #South Transylvania
			add_state_core = 84        #South Transylvania
			transfer_state = 806    #Maramures
			add_state_core = 806    #Maramures
			transfer_state = 807    #Northern Partium
			add_state_core = 807    #Northern Partium
		}
		if = { limit = { 76 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 76 }                #North Transylvania
		76 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #North Transylvania
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { owns_state = 819 } }    #Szeklerland
			if = { limit = { 819 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 819 }                #Szeklerland
			819 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Szeklerland
		}
		if = { limit = { 82 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 82 }                #Banat
		82 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Banat
		if = { limit = { 83 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 83 }                #Southern Partium
		83 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Southern Partium
		if = { limit = { 84 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 84 }                #South Transylvania
		84 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #South Transylvania
		if = { limit = { 806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 806 }                #Maramures
		806 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Maramures
		if = { limit = { 807 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 807 }                #Northern Partium
		807 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Northern Partium
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRA
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = TRA }
		}
	}

	#Set up Transylvania as a puppet state, but keep Banat and the Partium.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.148.c
		TRA = {
			transfer_state = 76        #North Transylvania
			add_state_core = 76        #North Transylvania
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { owns_state = 819 } }    #Szeklerland
				transfer_state = 819    #Szeklerland
				add_state_core = 819    #Szeklerland
			}
			transfer_state = 84        #South Transylvania
			add_state_core = 84        #South Transylvania
			transfer_state = 806    #Maramures
			add_state_core = 806    #Maramures
		}
		if = { limit = { 76 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 76 }                #North Transylvania
		76 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #North Transylvania
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { owns_state = 819 } }    #Szeklerland
			if = { limit = { 819 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 819 }                #Szeklerland
			819 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Szeklerland
		}
		if = { limit = { 84 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 84 }                #South Transylvania
		84 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #South Transylvania
		if = { limit = { 806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 806 }                #Maramures
		806 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Maramures
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRA
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = { puppet = TRA }
		}
	}
}

# Encroachment on adriatic waters
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.151
	title = hungary_flavor.151.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.151.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		any_owned_state = { is_coastal = yes }
		has_country_flag = HUN_adriatic_initiative_enabled
		NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
		any_country = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			has_war_with = ITA
			ships_in_area = { area = 168 size > 0 }
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	# We will honor the treaty.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.151.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				has_war_with = ITA
				ships_in_area = { area = 168 size > 0 }
			}
			HUN = { declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = puppet_wargoal_focus } }
		}
		ITA = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ita.10 } }
	}

	# I suppose we could just ignore those ships.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.151.b
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = HUN_adriatic_initiative_opinion }
		clr_country_flag = HUN_adriatic_initiative_enabled
		effect_tooltip = {
			ITA = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_adriatic_initiative_opinion }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_dishonored_adriatic_initiative }
						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					target = ROOT
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
		}
		ITA = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_ita.11 } }
	}
}

						83        #Southern Partium
						84        #South Transylvania
						810        #Maramures
						807        #South Bucovina
					}
				}
				else = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ROM
						type = take_state_focus
						generator = {
							76        #North Transylvania
							810        #Szeklerland
							82        #Banat
							83        #Southern Partium
							84        #South Transylvania
							810        #Maramures
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {

		}
		if = {
			limit = { CZE = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_CZE_accepts_danube_federation
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_CZE_declines_danube_federation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { YUG = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_YUG_accepts_danube_federation
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_YUG_declines_danube_federation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_ROM_accepts_danube_federation
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_ROM_declines_danube_federation }
		}
	}

	# We will immediately start supporting the agreeing parties.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.170.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AUS = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				CZE = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				YUG = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				ROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { AUS = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			AUS = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					add_ideas = underground_communism
					news_event = { id = hun_news.19 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CZE = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					add_ideas = underground_communism
					news_event = { id = hun_news.19 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { YUG = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			YUG = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					add_ideas = underground_communism
					news_event = { id = hun_news.19 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation } }
			ROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					add_ideas = underground_communism
					news_event = { id = hun_news.19 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# They have misguided visions of the future of the revolution.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.170.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AUS = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				CZE = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				YUG = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
				ROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation }
			}
		}
	}
}

		if = {

			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1936.3.31"
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1936.12.31
				date < 1938.1.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1937.3.31"
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1937.12.31
				date < 1939.1.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1938.3.31"
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date > 1938.12.31
				date < 1940.1.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				last_election = "1939.3.31"
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = amphibious_mechanized_bonus
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			technology = amphibious_mechanized_infantry
		}
	}

	# Fascinating, but ultimately of little use to us.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.200.b
		add_war_support = -0.01
	}
}

# Edward VIII Becomes King of [ENG.GetNameDef]
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.202
	title = hungary_flavor.202.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.202.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		has_idea = king_edward_of_windsor
		ENG = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" }
				has_idea = ENG_king_edward_fascism
				has_idea = ENG_king_edward
			}
		}
	}

	# Turn towards the Swedish royalty.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.202.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = SWE }
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties }
		ENG = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties } }
		remove_ideas = king_edward_of_windsor
		if = {
			limit = {
				SWE = { exists = yes }
				SWE = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SWE modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SWE modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties }
		}
		add_ideas = king_carl_wilhelm
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hun_news.16 } }
	}

	# Submit to the rule of Edward and the English.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.202.b
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = ENG
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		ENG = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = HUN
					autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
					freedom_level = 0.5
				}
				else = { puppet = HUN }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { hours = 6  id = hun_news.44 } }
	}

	# Abolish the monarchy.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.202.c
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = SWE
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.05
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties }
		ENG = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_dynastic_ties } }
		remove_ideas = king_edward_of_windsor
	}
}

# Slovakia votes no on plebiscite
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor.207
	title = hungary_flavor.207.t
	desc = hungary_flavor.207.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Maybe they are better off governed indirectly.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.207.a
		trigger = {
			SLO = { exists = no }
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		SLO = {
			add_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
			transfer_state = 70        #Western Slovakia
			add_state_core = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			transfer_state = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { owns_state = 818 } } # Sobrance
				add_state_core = 818    #Sobrance
				transfer_state = 818    #Sobrance
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SLO
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}
			else = {
				puppet = SLO
			}
		}
	}

	# It is an unfortunate result. Perhaps in time they will see reason.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor.207.b
	}
}

# Slovenia for Adriatic ports (event for ITA)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ita.1
	title = hungary_flavor_ita.1.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_ita.1.d_fiume
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_fiume }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_ita.1.d_zara
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_ita.1.d_both
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara_and_fiume }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ita.1.a
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_slovenia_threat }
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy } }
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy } }
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara_and_fiume }
			effect_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					transfer_state = 163    #Zara
					transfer_state = 801    #Fiume
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara }
			effect_tooltip = { FROM = { transfer_state = 163 } }    #Zara
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_fiume }
			effect_tooltip = { FROM = { transfer_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_partition.25 } }
		}
	}
	#Decline
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ita.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara_and_fiume
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				HUN = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				HUN = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_partition.26 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_zara
		}
	}
}

# Hungarian deal
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_ita.2
	title = hungary_flavor_ita.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_ita.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_military_support
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_political_support
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_fiume_plus
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_zara_plus
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.6
				has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_istria_plus
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_ita.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_hungarys_conditions_colon
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_non_aggression_pact }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = HUN relation = non_aggression_pact }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_military_support }
				HUN = { send_equipment = { target = ROOT type = infantry_equipment amount = 10000 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_political_support }
				HUN = { add_timed_idea = { idea = supporting_italy days = 548 } }
				ROOT = { add_timed_idea = { idea = support_from_hungary days = 548 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_fiume_plus }
				HUN = { transfer_state = 801 }    #Fiume
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_zara_plus }
				HUN = { transfer_state = 163 }    #Zara
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_ITA_negotiation_istria_plus }
				HUN = { transfer_state = 736 }    #Istria
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.27 } }
	}
	#Decline
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_ita.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.28 } }
	}
}

add_namespace = hun_news

# The partition of Yugoslavia
news_event = {
	id = hun_news.1
	title = hun_news.1.t
	desc = hun_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_009

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_end_of_yugoslavian_partition
			clr_country_flag = HUN_is_partitioning_YUG
			if = {
				limit = {
					YUG = { exists = no }
					tag = HUN
				}
				annex_country = { target = YUG transfer_troops = no }
			}
		}
	}

	#The new borders look nice.
	option = {
		name = hun_news.1.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = HUN
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition
				AND = {
					tag = SER
					is_puppet_of = HUN
				}
				AND = {
					tag = BUL
					owns_state = 106    #Macedonia
				}
				AND = {
					tag = ALB
					owns_state = 105    #Montenegro
				}
				AND = {
					tag = ITA
					OR = {
						owns_state = 105    #Montenegro
						owns_state = 805    #Ljubljana
						owns_state = 103    #Dalmatia
					}
				}
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					owns_state = 102    #Slovenia
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = HUN }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition5 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_given_territory5 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition4 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_given_territory4 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition3 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_given_territory3 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition2 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_given_territory2 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition1 }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_given_territory1 }
			}
		}
	}
	#The peace of Europe is in danger!
	option = {
		name = hun_news.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ENG = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_government = democratic
					}
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
				tag = YUG
				tag = ROM
				tag = GRE
			}
		}
	}
	#Amazing, how quickly countries appear, and vanish.
	option = {
		name = hun_news.1.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = HUN
				is_puppet_of = HUN
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				has_country_flag = HUN_received_territory_during_partition
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {

				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus

			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hun_news.4.d_CZE
		trigger = {
			HUN = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_news_event_generic_read_write

			}
		}
	}
	#We are wise to stay out of this
	option = {

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tag = CZE
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = POL
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#This is mildly interesting
	option = {
		name = hun_news.4.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = HUN
				tag = CZE
				tag = POL
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
	#Maybe this will stabilize the region

		name = hun_news.4.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = HUN
				tag = CZE
				tag = POL
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = hun_news.44
	title = hun_news.44.t
	desc = hun_news.44.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_royal_visit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes

	#Long may this new union last.
	option = {
		name = hun_news.44.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = HUN
				tag = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
			}
		}
	}

	#It would seem that Hungary is not destined for self-rule.
	option = {
		name = hun_news.44.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = HUN
				tag = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
			}
		}
	}
}

#########################
#PARTITION OF YUGOSLAVIA#
#########################

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_partition

# The Partition of Yugoslavia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.1
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_country_flag = HUN_is_partitioning_YUG }

	#A fruitful agreement
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.1.a
		transfer_state = 45        #Novi Sad
		transfer_state = 868    #Prekmurje
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_one_unit_of_volunteer_corps
		hidden_effect = {
			load_oob = YUG_to_HUN_volunteer_corps
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.2 }

			#ROOT has been a badboy
			add_to_variable = { var = global.HUN_badboy_rating value = 1 }
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
					has_country_flag = HUN_policing_expansion_of_hungary
				}
				hidden_effect = { worsen_relations_with_HUN = yes }
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_their_opinion_of_us_will_deteriorate
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.4 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# The fate of Slavonia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.2
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We will have it back.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.2.a
		add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = HUN_annexed_slavonia_threat }
		transfer_state = 109    #Slavonia
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.3 } }
	}

	#Croatia will become our puppet.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.2.b
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_puppeted_slavonia_threat }
		CRO = { transfer_state = 109 }    #Slavonia
		puppet = CRO
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.3 } }
		if = { limit = { 109 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 109 }                #Slavonia
		109 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slavonia
	}

	#Croatia will become independent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.2.c
		CRO = { transfer_state = 109 }    #Slavonia
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.3 } }
		if = { limit = { 109 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 109 }                #Slavonia
		109 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slavonia
	}
}

# The fate of Croatia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.3
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.3.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it, just like Slavonia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.3.a
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 109    #Slavonia
		}
		transfer_state = 803    #Croatia
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_coastal_croatia_threat }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.4 } }
	}

	#Give it back to Croatia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.3.b
		trigger = {
			CRO = {
				exists = yes
				owns_state = 109    #Slavonia
			}
		}
		CRO = {
			transfer_state = 803    #Croatia
			set_capital = {
				state = 803 #Croatia
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.4 } }
		if = { limit = { 803 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 803 }                #Croatia
		803 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Croatia
	}
}


# The fate of Pag
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.4
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.4.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.4.a
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 803    #Croatia
		}
		transfer_state = 813    #Pag
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_coastal_croatia_threat }
		hidden_effect = {
			#ship "transfer"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHU }
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_DNF }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
					load_oob = YUG_to_HUN_ship_transfer
					else = {
						load_oob = YUG_to_HUN_ship_transfer_legacy
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_AHU
						has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_DNF
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
					load_oob = YUG_to_AHU_ship_transfer
					else = {
						load_oob = YUG_to_AHU_ship_transfer_legacy
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.5 }
		}
	}

	#Give it back to Croatia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.4.b
		trigger = {
			CRO = {
				exists = yes
				owns_state = 803    #Croatia
			}
		}
		CRO = { transfer_state = 813 }    #Pag
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.5 } }
		if = { limit = { 813 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 813 }                #Pag
		813 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Pag
	}

	#Give it to Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.4.c
		ITA = {
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_coastal_croatia_threat }
			transfer_state = 813    #Pag
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.5 }
			ITA = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 813 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 813 }                #Pag
		813 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Pag
	}
}

# The fate of Serbia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.5
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.5.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.5.a
		add_named_threat = { threat = 6 name = HUN_annexed_serbia_threat }
		transfer_state = 107    #Serbia
		transfer_state = 108    #Morava
		transfer_state = 45    #Panceva
		#transfer_state = 799	#Srem
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.6 } }
	}
	#Create a Serbian puppet state
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.5.b
		add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = HUN_puppeted_serbia_threat }
		SER = {
			transfer_state = 107    #Serbia
			transfer_state = 108    #Morava
		}
		puppet = SER
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.6 } }
		if = { limit = { 107 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 107 }                #Serbia
		107 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Serbia
		if = { limit = { 108 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 108 }                #Morava
		108 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Morava
	}
	#Liberate Serbia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.5.c
		SER = {
			transfer_state = 107    #Serbia
			transfer_state = 108    #Morava
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.6 } }
		if = { limit = { 107 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 107 }                #Serbia
		107 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Serbia
		if = { limit = { 108 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 108 }                #Morava
		108 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Morava
	}
}

# The fate of Bosnia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.6
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.6.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.6.a
		trigger = {
			104 = { #Bosnia
				any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 2 name = HUN_annexed_bosnia_threat }
		transfer_state = 104    #Bosnia
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.7 } }
	}

	#Give it to Serbia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.6.b
		trigger = { SER = { exists = yes } }
		SER = {
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_bosnia_threat }
			transfer_state = 104    #Bosnia
			add_state_core = 104    #Bosnia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.7 }
			SER = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes    #Bosnia is big enough to be worth 2 flags
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 104 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 104 }                #Bosnia
		104 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Bosnia
	}

	#Give it to Croatia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.6.c
		trigger = { CRO = { exists = yes } }
		CRO = {
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_bosnia_threat }
			transfer_state = 104    #Bosnia
			add_state_core = 104    #Bosnia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.7 }
			CRO = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes    #Bosnia is big enough to be worth 2 flags
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 104 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 104 }                #Bosnia
		104 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Bosnia
	}

	#Liberate Bosnia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.6.e
		BOS = {
			transfer_state = 104    #Bosnia
			add_state_core = 104    #Bosnia
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.7 } }
		if = { limit = { 104 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 104 }                #Bosnia
		104 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Bosnia
	}
}

# The fate of Torontal
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.8
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.8.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#It belongs to us.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.8.a
		transfer_state = 45    #Torontal
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.9 } }
	}

	#Serbia can have it.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.8.b
		trigger = {
			SER = { exists = yes }
		}
		SER = { transfer_state = 45 }    #Torontal
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.9 } }
		if = { limit = { 45 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 45 }                #Torontal
		45 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Torontal
	}

	#Actually, let Romania have it.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.8.c
		trigger = {
			ROM = {
				exists = yes
				owns_state = 82    #Banat
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			transfer_state = 45    #Torontal
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ROM = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.9 }
		}
		if = { limit = { 45 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 45 }                #Torontal
		45 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Torontal
	}
}

# The fate of Macedonia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.10
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.10.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.10.a
		trigger = {
			106 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_macedonia_threat }

		if = {
			limit = {
				BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			BUL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_betrayed_promises } }
		}
		transfer_state = 106    #Macedonia
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.11 } }
	}

	#It belongs to Serbia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.10.b
		trigger = {
			SER = { exists = yes }
			106 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SER } }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			BUL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_betrayed_promises } }
		}
		SER = {
			transfer_state = 106    #Macedonia
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.11 } }
		if = { limit = { 106 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 106 }                #Macedonia
		106 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Macedonia
	}

	#Give it to Bulgaria
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.10.c
		trigger = {

	}

country_event = {

		}

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.12 } }
		if = { limit = { 810 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 810 }                #Tetovo
		810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Tetovo
	}

	#Give it to Albania
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.11.b
		trigger = {
			810 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ALB } }    #Tetovo
		}
		ALB = {
			transfer_state = 810    #Tetovo
			add_state_core = 810    #Tetovo
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.12 }
			ALB = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 810 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 810 }                #Tetovo
		810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Tetovo
	}

	#Give it to Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.11.c
		trigger = {
			810 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ITA } }    #Tetovo
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 810    #Tetovo
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.12 }
			ITA = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 810 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 810 }                #Tetovo
		810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Tetovo
	}

	#Give it to Bulgaria
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.11.e
		trigger = {
			106 = { is_owned_by = BUL }    #Macedonia
		}
		BUL = {
			transfer_state = 810    #Tetovo
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.12 }
			BUL = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 810 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 810 }                #Tetovo
		810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Tetovo
	}

	#Give it to Serbia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.11.f
		trigger = {
			106 = { is_owned_by = SER }    #Macedonia
		}
		SER = { transfer_state = 810 }    #Tetovo

# The fate of Montenegro
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.13
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.13.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.13.a
		trigger = {
			105 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_montenegro_threat }
		transfer_state = 105    #Montenegro
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.14 } }
	}

	#It belongs to Serbia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.13.b
		trigger = {
			SER = { exists = yes }
			105 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = SER } }
		}
		SER = {
			transfer_state = 105    #Montenegro
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_montenegro_threat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.14 }
			SER = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 105 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 105 }                #Montenegro
		105 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Montenegro
	}

	#Give it to Albania
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.13.c
		trigger = {
			ALB = { exists = yes }
			44 = { is_owned_by = ALB }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			ALB = { country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor_alb.1 } }
		}
		ALB = {
			transfer_state = 105    #Montenegro
			add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_montenegro_threat }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.14 }
			ALB = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 105 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 105 }                #Montenegro
		105 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Montenegro
	}

	#Give it to Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.13.e
		trigger = {
			ITA = { exists = yes }
			44 = { is_owned_by = ITA }
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 105    #Montenegro
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.14 }
			ITA = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
		}
		if = { limit = { 105 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 105 }                #Montenegro
		105 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Montenegro
	}

	#Liberate Montenegro
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.13.f
		MNT = {
			transfer_state = 105    #Montenegro
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.14 } }
		if = { limit = { 105 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 105 }                #Montenegro
		105 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Montenegro
	}
}

# The fate of Kotor
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.15
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.15.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.15.a
		trigger = {
			808 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }    #Kotor
		}
		transfer_state = 808    #Kotor
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 163 } }    #Zara
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.16 }
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
						country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.17 }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 736 } }    #Istria
								country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.18 }
								else = {
									if = {
										limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 809 } }    #Primorska
										country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.19 }
										else = {
											if = {
												limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 805 } }        #Ljubljana
												country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.20 }
												else = {
													if = {
														limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 102 } }    #Slovenia
														country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
														else = {
															#end of negotiation
															news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Give it to Montenegro
	option = {

					if = {
						limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
						country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.17 }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 736 } }    #Istria
								country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.18 }
								else = {
									if = {
										limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 809 } }    #Primorska
										country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.19 }
										else = {
											if = {
												limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 805 } }        #Ljubljana
												country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.20 }
												else = {
													if = {
														limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 102 } }    #Slovenia
														country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
														else = {
															#end of negotiation
															news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 808 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 808 }                #Kotor
		808 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Kotor
	}

		name = hungary_flavor_partition.16.a

			163 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }    #Zara
		}
		transfer_state = 163    #Zara
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 801 } }    #Fiume
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.17 }
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 736 } }    #Istria
						country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.18 }
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 809 } }    #Primorska
								country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.19 }
								else = {
									if = {
										limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 805 } }        #Ljubljana
										country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.20 }
										else = {
											if = {
												limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 102 } }    #Slovenia
												country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
												else = {
													#end of negotiation
													news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Give it to Croatia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.16.b
		trigger = {
			163 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = CRO } }    #Zara
		}
		CRO = {
			transfer_state = 163    #Zara
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}

				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.17 }

									}
								}

			CRO = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			if = { limit = { 163 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 163 }                #Zara
			163 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Zara
		}
	}

	#Give it to Serbia

		trigger = {
			ITA = { exists = yes }
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 163    #Zara
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {

								else = {

	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.17.d

# The fate of Slovenia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.20
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.20.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }    #Slovenia
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
		transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
		hidden_effect = {
			#end of negotiation
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
		}
	}

	#Give it to Austria
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }    #Slovenia
			}
			AUS = { NOT = { owns_state = 810 } }    #Burgenland
		}
		AUS = {
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#end of negotiation
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			AUS = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
		805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Make a deal with Austria
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }    #Slovenia
			}
			AUS = { owns_state = 810 }    #Burgenland
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_partition.20.c.tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_austria
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.24 } }
	}

	#Give it to Germany
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER } }    #Slovenia
			}
			NOT = { 805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } } }    #Ljubljana
			NOT = { 102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } } }    #Slovenia
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#end of negotiation
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			GER = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
		805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Give it to Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER } }    #Slovenia
			}
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 163    #Zara
						owns_state = 801    #Fiume
					}
					has_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_zara
				}
			}
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#end of negotiation
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			ITA = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
		805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Make a deal with Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				805 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ITA } }    #Ljubljana
				102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ITA } }    #Slovenia
			}
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 163    #Zara
					owns_state = 801    #Fiume
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_zara }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_partition.20.g.tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.23 } }
	}

	#Liberate Slovenia
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.h
		SLV = {
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
		805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
		hidden_effect = {
			#end of negotiation
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			SLV = {
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
				add_received_territory_flag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#Decide for the northern and southern parts separately
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.20.i
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_partition.20.i.tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_slovenia_split_decision
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.21 } }
	}
}


# The fate of Northern Slovenia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.21
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.21.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Annex it.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.a
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }    #Slovenia
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = HUN_annexed_slovenia_threat }
		transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 } }
	}

	#Give it to Germany
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.b
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = GER } }     #Slovenia
			NOT = { 102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } } }     #Slovenia
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
		}
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Give it to Austria.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.c
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }
			AUS = { NOT = { owns_state = 810 } }    #Burgenland
		}
		AUS = {
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
		}
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Make a deal with Austria
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.e
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = AUS } }
			AUS = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_burgenland }
				owns_state = 810    #Burgenland
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_partition.21.e.tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_austria
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.24 } }
	}

	#Give it to Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.f
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ITA } }
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 163    #Zara
						owns_state = 801    #Fiume
					}
					has_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_zara
				}
			}
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
		}
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Make a deal with Italy
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.g
		trigger = {
			102 = { any_neighbor_state = { is_owned_by = ITA } }
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 163    #Zara
					owns_state = 801    #Fiume
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = refused_slovenia_for_zara }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_partition.21.g.tt
		set_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.23 } }
	}

	#Give it to the Slovenes.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.21.h
		SLV = {
			transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_look_favorably_on_this_decision
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SLV = { add_received_territory_flag = yes }
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
		}
		if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
	}
}

# A deal with Italy
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.23
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.23.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We don't ask for anything in return.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.23.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy } }
				ITA = {
					transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
					add_received_territory_flag = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy } } }
					country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy } }
				ITA = {
					transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
					add_received_territory_flag = yes
				}
				#end of negotiation
				news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	#We want Fiume
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.23.b
		trigger = {
			ITA = { owns_state = 801 }    #Fiume
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_fiume
				country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_ita.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	#We want Zara
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.23.c
		trigger = {
			ITA = { owns_state = 163 }    #Zara
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara
				country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_ita.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	#We want Zara and Fiume
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.23.e
		trigger = {
			ITA = {
				owns_state = 163    #Zara
				owns_state = 801    #Fiume
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara_and_fiume
				country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_ita.1 }
			}
		}
	}
}


# A deal with Austria
country_event = {

	title = hungary_flavor_partition.24.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	#We don't ask for anything in return.
	option = {

			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_austria } }
				AUS = {
					transfer_state = 102    #Slovenia
					add_received_territory_flag = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria } } }
					country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
				}
				if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
				102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria } }
				AUS = {
					transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
					add_received_territory_flag = yes
				}
				if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
				805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
				#end of negotiation
				news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	#We want Burgenland
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.24.b
		trigger = {
			AUS = { owns_state = 810 }    #Burgenland
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_burgenland
				country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_aus.3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Italy accepts (Slovenia/Ljubljana for Adriatic ports)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.25
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.25.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Splendid
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.25.a
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara_and_fiume } }
			transfer_state = 163    #Zara
			transfer_state = 801    #Fiume
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_zara } }
			transfer_state = 163    #Zara
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { has_country_flag = HUN_hungary_wants_fiume } }
			transfer_state = 801    #Fiume
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy } }
			if = { limit = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 805 }                #Ljubljana
			805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Ljubljana
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy } }
			if = { limit = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 102 }                #Slovenia
			102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_claim_forbidden clr_state_flag = HUN_is_claimed_by_HUN }    #Slovenia
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { YUG = { owns_state = 805 } }    #Ljubljana
				country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
				else = {
					#end of negotiation
					news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Italy declines (Slovenia/Ljubljana for Adriatic ports)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_partition.26
	title = hungary_flavor_partition.26.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_partition.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Strange
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_partition.26.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy
			}
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.20 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy }
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy
			}
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.21 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_italy
				NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_italy }
			}
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_partition.22 }
		}
	}
}

# Hungarian Alliance (event for Poland upon faction invite)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_pol.1
	title = hungary_flavor_pol.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_pol.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_pol.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_invited_to_faction }
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.7 hours = 6 }
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_pol.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.8 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

# Austria-Hungary offers Guarantees for Krakow and Galicia (event for POL)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_pol.2
	title = hungary_flavor_pol.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_pol.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Cede the territories in question
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 0.8
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {

# Hungary demands Translyvania (event for ROM)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_rom.1
	title = hungary_flavor_rom.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_rom.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Cede Transylvania
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FROM = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_realism
					NOT = { has_army_manpower = { size > 499999 } }
				}
			}
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 599999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 699999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 799999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 899999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 999999 } } }
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.1.a
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.21 } }
		news_event = { hours = 6 id = hun_news.28 }
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.22 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				transfer_state = 83        #Grisana
				transfer_state = 84        #Transylvania
				transfer_state = 76        #North Transylvania
				transfer_state = 819    #Szeklerland
				transfer_state = 806    #Maramaros
				transfer_state = 807    #Northern Partium
			}
		}
	}

	#We will issue a counterdemand!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_state_claim = 154    #Alfld
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { owns_state = 45 } } #Torontal
			add_state_claim = 45    #Torontal
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_demanded_territory }
			country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.20 }
		}
	}

	#They can have the northern parts.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.1.e
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 76        #North Transylvania
			owns_state = 819    #Szeklerland
			owns_state = 806    #Maramaros
			owns_state = 807    #Northern Partium
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				transfer_state = 76        #North Transylvania
				transfer_state = 819    #Szeklerland
				transfer_state = 806    #Maramaros
				transfer_state = 807    #Northern Partium
			}
			country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.19 }
		}
	}
}

			HUN = { is_ahu = yes }
		}
	}

		text = hungary_flavor_rom.5.d_2

			HUN = { is_not_ahu = yes }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_little_entente

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = CZE value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = CZE value > 24 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						CZE = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = democratic
						CZE = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = fascism
						CZE = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = communism
						CZE = { has_government = communism }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				AND = {
					has_government = neutrality
					CZE = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				}
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.5.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_rom.5.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = { set_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_plus }

				limit = { CZE = { OR = { has_country_flag = little_entente_CZE_plus has_country_flag = little_entente_CZE_minus } } }

			}
		}
	}

	#Tell them to leave us out of their petty alliance
	option = {
