			factor = 60
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.5.b
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = { set_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_minus }
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { OR = { has_country_flag = little_entente_CZE_plus has_country_flag = little_entente_CZE_minus } } }
				CZE = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_cze.6 } }
			}
		}
	}

			}
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 599999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 699999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 799999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 899999 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.1 FROM = { has_army_manpower = { size > 999999 } } }
		}
		HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.132 } }
		BUL = {
			country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_bul.5 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				transfer_state = 77        #Southern Dobrudja
				transfer_state = 814    #Northern Dobrudja
			}
		}
	}

	#We won't give an inch.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.8.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.133 }
			effect_tooltip = {
						create_wargoal = {			
				expire = 100
					type = take_state_focus
					target = ROM
					generator = { 77 805 }
				}
			}
		}
		BUL = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_bul.6 } }

	}
}

			}

				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 74 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 99 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.167 } }
		SZE = { transfer_state = 819 }    #Szeklerland
		if = { limit = { 819 = { is_core_of = ROOT } } remove_state_core = 819 }                #Szeklerland
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SZE
				autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				freedom_level = 0.5
			}

		}
	}

	#What next? The whole of Transylvania? I think not.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_rom.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}

# [HUN.GetName] attacks Romania
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_sov.6
	title = hungary_flavor_sov.6.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_sov.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = SOV
		NOT = { has_war_with = ROM }
		HUN = { has_war_with = ROM }
		has_global_flag = HUN_SOV_romanian_partition_agreed
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	# Commence the attack. We will crush Romania from two sides.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_sov.6.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROM } }
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { is_ahu = yes } }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROM
					type = take_state_focus
					generator = {
						78        #Bessarabia
						79        #Moldova
					}
				}
				else = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ROM
						type = take_state_focus
						generator = {
							78        #Bessarabia
							79        #Moldova
							80        #North Bucovina
							807        #South Bucovina
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		name = hungary_flavor_sze.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}

		OR = {
			76 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #North Transylvania
			82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Banat
			83 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Southern Partium
			84 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Transylvania
			806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Maramaros
			807 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Northern Partium
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_transylvania }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_transylvania }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			76 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #North Transylvania
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Banat
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			83 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Southern Partium
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			84 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Transylvania
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Maramaros
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			807 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Northern partium
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.2.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_transylvania days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 76 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #North Transylvania
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			76 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #North Transylvania
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Banat
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			82 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Banat
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 83 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Southern Partium
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			83 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Southern Partium
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 84 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Transylvania
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			84 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Transylvania
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Maramaros
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			806 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Maramaros
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 807 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Northern Partium
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			807 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Northern Partium
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.2.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_transylvania days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_transylvania_will_slow_down
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decision)
# Acquisition of Banat
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.10
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.10.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	tag = HUN
	#	owns_state = 82		#Banat
	#	82 = {
	#		NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned }
	#	}
	#
	#	NOT = { 82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 0
	#}

	#We will start the integration process.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.10.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_start
		add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		add_state_core = 82        #Banat
		hidden_effect = { 82 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#The state is fine as it is.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.10.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_state_will_not_be_integrated
		hidden_effect = { 82 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Banat
	}
}

# Banat lost
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.11
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.11.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { owns_state = 82 }        #Banat

		82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.11.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 82        #Banat
		hidden_effect = { 82 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

# Banat integrated

	title = hungary_flavor_territory.12.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 82        #Banat

		82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 86    #96*0.9 due to existing Hungarian population
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_transylvania
		}
	}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.12.a
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		hidden_effect = { 82 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

# Rebellion in Banat
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.13
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.13.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 82        #Banat

		82 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_transylvanian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_transylvania
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.13.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		TRA = { transfer_state = 82 }    #Banat
		remove_state_core = 82            #Banat
		hidden_effect = { 82 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.13.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_transylvanian_rebels days = 100 }
		82 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Banat
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.13.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 82        #Banat
		hidden_effect = {
			82 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

	#		NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned }
	#	}
	#
	#	NOT = { 806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 0
	#}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.40.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_start
		add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		add_state_core = 806        #Maramaros
		hidden_effect = { 806 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#The state is fine as it is.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.40.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_state_will_not_be_integrated
		hidden_effect = { 806 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Maramaros
	}
}

# Maramaros lost

	id = hungary_flavor_territory.41
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.41.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.41.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { owns_state = 806 }    #Maramaros

		806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.41.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 806        #Maramaros
		hidden_effect = { 806 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_transylvania
		}
	}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.42.a
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		hidden_effect = { 806 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

# Rebellion in Maramaros
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.43
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.43.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_transylvania

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 806        #Maramaros

		806 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_transylvanian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_transylvania
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.43.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		TRA = { transfer_state = 806 }    #Maramaros
		remove_state_core = 806            #Maramaros
		hidden_effect = { 806 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.43.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_transylvanian_rebels days = 100 }
		806 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Maramaros
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.43.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 806        #Maramaros
		hidden_effect = {
			806 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of Slovakia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.101
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.101.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 70		#Western Slovakia
	#			NOT = { 70 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Western Slovakia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 71		#Eastern Slovakia
	#			NOT = { 71 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Eastern Slovakia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 73		#Carpathian Ruthenia
	#			NOT = { 73 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Carpathian Ruthenia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 818		#Sobrance
	#			NOT = { 818 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Sobrance
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.101.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_slovakia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 70 }        #Western Slovakia
				70 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 71 }        #Eastern Slovakia
				71 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 71        #Eastern Slovakia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 73 }        #Carpathian Ruthenia
				73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 73        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 818 }        #Sobrance
				73 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 818        #Sobrance
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.101.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_slovakia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.101.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.101 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Slovakian region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.102
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.102.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Western Slovakia
			71 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Eastern Slovakia
			73 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Carpathian Ruthenia
			818 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Sobrance
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovakia }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_slovakia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Western Slovakia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			71 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Eastern Slovakia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			73 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			818 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Sobrance
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.102.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovakia days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Western Slovakia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			70 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Western Slovakia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 71 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Eastern Slovakia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			71 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Eastern Slovakia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 73 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			73 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Carpathian Ruthenia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 818 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Sobrance
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			818 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Sobrance
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.102.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_slovakia days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_slovakia_will_slow_down
	}
}

	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.110.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_state_will_not_be_integrated
		hidden_effect = { 70 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Western Slovakia
	}
}

# Western Slovakia lost
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.111
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.111.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.111.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { owns_state = 70 }    #Western Slovakia

		70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.111.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
		70 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}
}

# Western Slovakia integrated
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.112
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.112.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.112.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 70        #Western Slovakia

		70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 86            #96*0.9 due to existing Hungarian population
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
	}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.112.a
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		hidden_effect = { 70 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

# Rebellion in Western Slovakia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.113
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.113.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.113.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_southern_slovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 70        #Western Slovakia

		70 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_slovakian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovakia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.113.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		SLO = { transfer_state = 70 }    #Western Slovakia
		remove_state_core = 70            #Western Slovakia
		hidden_effect = { 70 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.113.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_slovakian_rebels days = 100 }
		70 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Western Slovakia
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.113.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 70        #Western Slovakia
		hidden_effect = {
			70 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovakia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.143.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		SLO = { transfer_state = 818 }    #Sobrance
		remove_state_core = 818            #Sobrance
		hidden_effect = { 818 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.143.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_slovakian_rebels days = 100 }
		818 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Sobrance
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.143.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 818        #Sobrance
		hidden_effect = {
			818 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = hungary_flavor_territory.201.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.201.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#	tag = HUN

	#		AND = {

	#			owns_state = 808		#Kotor

	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.201.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_croatia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 109 }        #Slavonia
				109 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 109        #Slavonia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 801 }        #Fiume
				801 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 801        #Fiume
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 803 }        #Croatia
				803 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 803        #Croatia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 813 }        #Pag
				808 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 813        #Pag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 163    #Zara
					is_ahu = yes
				}
				163 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_state_core = 163        #Zara
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 103    #Dalmatia
					is_ahu = yes
				}
				103 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 103        #Dalmatia
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 808    #Kotor
					is_ahu = yes
				}
				808 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 808        #Kotor
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.201.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_croatia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.201.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.201 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Croatian region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.202
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.202.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.202.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			109 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Slavonia
			801 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Fiume
			803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Croatia
			103 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Dalmatia
			808 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Kotor
			813 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Pag
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_croatia }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_croatia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			109 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Slavonia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			801 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Fiume
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Croatia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			103 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Dalmatia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			808 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Kotor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			813 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Pag
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.202.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_croatia days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 109 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Slavonia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			109 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Slavonia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 801 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Fiume
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			801 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Fiume
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Croatia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			803 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Croatia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 103 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Dalmatia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			103 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Dalmatia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 808 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Kotor
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			808 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Kotor
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 813 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Pag
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			813 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Pag
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.202.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_croatia days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_croatia_will_slow_down
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.213
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.213.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.213.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 109        #Slavonia

		109 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_croatia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}

			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes

	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.213.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels days = 100 }

	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels

		hidden_effect = { 803 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Croatia
	}
}

# Croatia lost
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.231
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.231.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.231.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { owns_state = 803 }    #Croatia

		803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.231.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 803        #Croatia
		803 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}
}

# Croatia integrated

	id = hungary_flavor_territory.232
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.232.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.232.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 803        #Croatia

		803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 96
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
	}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.232.a
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		hidden_effect = { 803 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

# Rebellion in Croatia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.233
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.233.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.233.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 803        #Croatia

		803 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_croatia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.233.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		CRO = { transfer_state = 803 }    #Croatia
		remove_state_core = 803            #Croatia
		hidden_effect = { 803 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.233.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels days = 100 }
		803 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Croatia
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.233.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 803        #Croatia
		hidden_effect = {
			803 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Rebellion in Dalmatia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.243
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.243.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.243.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 103        #Dalmatia
		owns_state = 163        #Zara

		103 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_croatia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.243.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		CRO = { transfer_state = 103 }    #Dalmatia
		CRO = { transfer_state = 163 }    #Zara
		remove_state_core = 103            #Dalmatia
		remove_state_core = 163            #Zara
		hidden_effect = { 103 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.243.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_croatian_rebels days = 100 }
		103 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Dalmatia
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.243.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 103        #Dalmatia
		remove_state_core = 163        #Zara
		hidden_effect = {
			103 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

	#			owns_state = 799		#Srem
	#			NOT = { 799 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Srem
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.301.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_vojvodina_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 45 }        #Torontal
				45 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 45        #Torontal
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.301.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_vojvodina_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.301.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.301 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Vojvodina region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.302
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.302.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.302.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			45 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Torontal

		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_vojvodina }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_vojvodina }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			45 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Torontal
		}

	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.302.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_vojvodina days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 45 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Torontal
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			45 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Torontal
		}

	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.302.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_vojvodina days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_vojvodina_will_slow_down
	}
}

# Rebellion in Torontal
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.313
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.313.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.313.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_partition

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 45        #Torontal

		45 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_vojvodina_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_vojvodina
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.313.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		SER = { transfer_state = 45 }    #Torontal
		remove_state_core = 45            #Torontal
		hidden_effect = { 45 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.313.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_vojvodina_rebels days = 100 }
		45 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Torontal
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.313.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 45        #Torontal
		hidden_effect = {
			45 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Burgenland region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.402
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.402.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_burgenland

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Burgenland
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_burgenland }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_burgenland }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Burgenland
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.402.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_burgenland days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Burgenland
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			810 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Burgenland
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.402.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_burgenland days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_burgenland_will_slow_down
	}
}

	#		NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned }
	#	}
	#
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 0
	#}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.410.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_start
		add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		add_state_core = 810        #Burgenland
		810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	#The state is fine as it is.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.410.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_state_will_not_be_integrated
		hidden_effect = { 810 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Burgenland
	}
}

# Burgenland lost
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.411
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.411.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.411.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_burgenland

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		NOT = { owns_state = 810 }    #Burgenland

		810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.411.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 810        #Burgenland
		810 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}
}

# Burgenland integrated
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.412
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.412.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.412.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_burgenland

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 810        #Burgenland

		810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 86            #96*0.9 due to existing Hungarian population
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
	}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.412.a
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		hidden_effect = { 810 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}
}

# Rebellion in Burgenland
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.413
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.413.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.413.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_burgenland

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 810        #Burgenland

		810 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_burgenland_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_burgenland
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.413.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		AUS = { transfer_state = 810 }    #Burgenland
		remove_state_core = 810            #Burgenland
		hidden_effect = { 810 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.413.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_burgenland_rebels days = 100 }
		810 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Burgenland
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.413.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 810        #Burgenland
		hidden_effect = {
			810 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of the Bohemian region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.501
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.501.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_czechoslovakia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 9		#Bohemia
	#			NOT = { 9 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Bohemia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 69		#Sudetenland
	#			NOT = { 69 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Sudetenland
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 74		#Eastern Sudetenland
	#			NOT = { 74 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Eastern Sudetenland
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 75		#Moravia
	#			NOT = { 75 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Moravia
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.501.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bohemia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 9 }        #Bohemia
				9 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 9        #Bohemia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 69 }        #Sudetenland
				69 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 69        #Sudetenland
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 74 }        #Eastern Sudetenland
				74 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 74        #Eastern Sudetenland
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 75 }    #Moravia
				75 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 75        #Moravia
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.501.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bohemia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.501.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.501 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Bohemian region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.502
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.502.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.502.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_czechoslovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			9 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Bohemia
			69 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Sudetenland
			74 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Eastern Sudetenland
			75 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Moravia
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bohemia }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bohemia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			9 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Bohemia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			69 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Sudetenland
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			74 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Eastern Sudetenland
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			75 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Moravia
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.502.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bohemia days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 9 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Bohemia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			9 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Bohemia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 69 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Sudetenland
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			69 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Sudetenland
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 74 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Eastern Sudetenland
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			74 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Eastern Sudetenland
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 75 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Moravia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			75 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Moravia
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.502.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bohemia days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_bohemia_will_slow_down
	}
}

# Rebellion in Eastern Sudetenland
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.533
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.533.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.533.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_czechoslovakia

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 74        #Eastern Sudetenland

		74 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_bohemian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bohemia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.533.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		CZE = { transfer_state = 74 }    #Eastern Sudetenland
		remove_state_core = 74            #Eastern Sudetenland
		hidden_effect = { 74 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.533.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_bohemian_rebels days = 100 }
		74 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Eastern Sudetenland
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.533.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 74        #Eastern Sudetenland
		hidden_effect = {
			74 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of the Galicia-Lodomeria region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.601
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.601.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.601.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 72		#Zalozie
	#			NOT = { 72 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Zalozie
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 88		#Krakow
	#			NOT = { 88 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Krakow
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 89		#Stanoslawow
	#			NOT = { 89 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Stanoslawow
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 91		#Lwow
	#			NOT = { 91 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Lwow
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.601.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_galicia_lodomeria_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 72 }        #Zalozie
				72 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 72        #Zalozie
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 88 }        #Krakow
				88 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 88        #Krakow
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 89 }        #Stanoslawow
				89 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 89        #Stanoslawow
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 91 }    #Lwow
				91 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 91        #Lwow
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.601.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_galicia_lodomeria_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.601.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.601 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Galicia-Lodomeria region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.602
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.602.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.602.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			72 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Zalozie
			88 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Krakow
			89 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Stanoslawow
			91 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Lwow
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_galicia_lodomeria }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_galicia_lodomeria }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			72 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Zalozie
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			88 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Krakow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			89 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Stanoslawow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			91 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Lwow
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.602.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_galicia_lodomeria days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 72 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Zalozie
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			72 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Zalozie
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 88 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Krakow
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			88 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Krakow
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 89 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Stanoslawow
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			89 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Stanoslawow
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 91 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Lwow
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			91 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Lwow
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.602.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_galicia_lodomeria days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_galicia_lodomeria_will_slow_down
	}
}

			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_galicia_lodomeria_rebels days = 100 }
		72 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Zalozie
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.613.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 72        #Zalozie
		hidden_effect = {
			72 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Rebellion in Krakow
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.623
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.623.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.623.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 88        #Krakow

		88 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_galicia_lodomeria_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_galicia_lodomeria
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.623.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		POL = { transfer_state = 88 }    #Krakow
		remove_state_core = 88            #Krakow
		hidden_effect = { 88 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.623.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_galicia_lodomeria_rebels days = 100 }
		88 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Krakow
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.623.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 88        #Krakow
		hidden_effect = {
			88 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of the Slovenia region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.701
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.701.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.701.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 102		#Slovenia
	#			NOT = { 102 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Slovenia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 805		#Ljubljana
	#			NOT = { 805 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Ljubljana
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.701.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_slovenia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 102 }        #Slovenia
				102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 102        #Slovenia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 805 }        #Ljubljana
				805 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 805        #Ljubljana
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.701.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_slovenia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.701.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.701 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Slovenia region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.702
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.702.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.702.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			102 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Slovenia
			805 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Ljubljana
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovenia }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_slovenia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			102 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Slovenia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			805 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Ljubljana
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.702.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovenia days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 102 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Slovenia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			102 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Slovenia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 805 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Ljubljana
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			805 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Ljubljana
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.702.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_slovenia days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_slovenia_will_slow_down
	}
}

	#	tag = HUN
	#	owns_state = 102 	#Slovenia
	#	102 = {
	#		NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	#		NOT = { has_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned }
	#	}
	#
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 0
	#}

	#Excellent.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.710.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_start
		add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		add_state_core = 102        #Slovenia
		102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	#The state is fine as it is.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.710.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_state_will_not_be_integrated
		hidden_effect = { 102 = { set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned } }        #Slovenia
	}
}

		102 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }

			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}

			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
	}

	#Excellent.

	}

# Rebellion in Slovenia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.713
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.713.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.713.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 102        #Slovenia

		102 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_slovenian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_slovenia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.713.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		SLV = { transfer_state = 102 }    #Slovenia
		remove_state_core = 102            #Slovenia
		hidden_effect = { 102 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.713.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_slovenian_rebels days = 100 }
		102 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Slovenia
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.713.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 102        #Slovenia
		hidden_effect = {
			102 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of the Istria & South Tirol region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.801
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.801.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.801.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 39		#South Tirol
	#			NOT = { 39 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#South Tirol
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 736		#Istria
	#			NOT = { 736 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Istria
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 809		#Gorizia
	#			NOT = { 809 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Gorizia
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 815		#Trieste
	#			NOT = { 815 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Trieste
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.801.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istria_south_tirol_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 39 }        #South Tirol
				39 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 39        #South Tirol
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 736 }        #Istria
				736 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 736        #Istria
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 809 }        #Gorizia
				809 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 809        #Gorizia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 815 }        #Trieste
				815 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 815        #Trieste
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.801.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_istria_south_tirol_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.801.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.801 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Istria & South Tirol region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.802
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.802.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.802.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		OR = {
			39 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #South Tirol
			736 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Istria
			809 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Gorizia
			815 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Trieste
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_istria_south_tirol }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_istria_south_tirol }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			39 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #South Tirol
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			736 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Istria
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			809 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Gorizia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			815 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Trieste
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.802.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_istria_south_tirol days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 39 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #South Tirol
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			39 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #South Tirol
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 736 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Istria
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			736 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Istria
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 809 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Gorizia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			809 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Gorizia
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 815 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Trieste
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			815 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Trieste
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.802.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_istria_south_tirol days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_istria_south_tirol_will_slow_down
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 39        #South Tirol
		hidden_effect = {
			39 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}

		modifier = {

			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
		}

			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
		}
	}

# Rebellion in Istria
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.823
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.823.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.823.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 736        #Istria

		736 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_istria_south_tirol_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_istria_south_tirol
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.823.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		ITA = { transfer_state = 736 }    #Istria
		remove_state_core = 736            #Istria
		hidden_effect = { 736 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.823.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_istria_south_tirol_rebels days = 100 }
		736 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Istria
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.823.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 736        #Istria
		hidden_effect = {
			736 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}
