# Deprecated (replaced by decisions)
# Integration of Bosnia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.901
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.901.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.901.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	owns_state = 104		#Bosnia
	#	NOT = { 104 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#Bosnia
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.901.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bosnia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 104 }        #Bosnia
				104 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 104        #Bosnia
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.901.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bosnia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.901.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.901 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Bosnian region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.902
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.902.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.902.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		104 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #Bosnia
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bosnia }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bosnia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			104 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #Bosnia
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.902.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bosnia days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 104 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #Bosnia
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			104 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Bosnia
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.902.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bosnia days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_bosnia_will_slow_down
	}
}

		104 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	#We will take it back eventually.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.911.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 104        #Bosnia
		104 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
	}
}

# Rebellion in Bosnia
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.913
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.913.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.913.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN
		owns_state = 104        #Bosnia

		104 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_bosnian_rebels }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 144
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bosnia
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_02
				has_country_flag = HUN_integration_bonus_01
			}
		}
	}

	#Let them go.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.913.a
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		BOS = { transfer_state = 104 }    #Bosnia
		remove_state_core = 104            #Bosnia
		hidden_effect = { 104 = { clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }
	}

	#Fight the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.913.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_continue
		random_list = {
			25 = { add_manpower = -1600 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -800 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -400 }
			25 = { add_manpower = -200 }
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_cracking_down_on_bosnian_rebels days = 100 }
		104 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #Bosnia
	}

	#Negotiate with the rebels
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.913.c
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_of_the_state_will_stop_indefinitely
		remove_05_conscription_resistance = yes
		remove_state_core = 104        #Bosnia
		hidden_effect = {
			104 = {
				clr_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated
				set_state_flag = HUN_integration_abandoned
			}
		}
	}
}

# Integration of Bucovina
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.1001
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.1001.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.1001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#trigger = {
	#	has_country_flag = HUN_can_integrate
	#	NOT = {    }
	#	tag = HUN
	#	is_ahu = yes
	#	OR = {
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 80		#North Bucovina
	#			NOT = { 80 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#North Bucovina
	#		}
	#		AND = {
	#			owns_state = 816		#South Bucovina
	#			NOT = { 816 = { is_core_of = ROOT } }	#South Bucovina
	#		}
	#	}
	#}

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 7
	#}

	#Integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.1001.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bosnia_will_be_gradually_integrated
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 80 }        #North Bucovina
				80 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 80        #North Bucovina
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 816 }        #South Bucovina
				816 = { set_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }
				add_05_conscription_resistance = yes
				add_state_core = 80        #North Bucovina
				add_state_core = 816    #South Bucovina
			}
		}
	}

	#Don't integrate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.1001.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_bosnia_will_remain_a_territory
	}

	#Decide later
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.1001.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_get_this_event_again
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { months = 6 id = hungary_flavor_territory.1001 } }
	}
}

# Resistance to integration in the Bucovina region
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_territory.1002
	title = hungary_flavor_territory.1002.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_territory.1002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_ahu_old

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		tag = HUN

		80 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }        #North Bucovina
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bucovina }
		NOT = { has_idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bucovina }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 24
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_01
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_country_flag = HUN_suppression_bonus_02
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			80 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #North Bucovina
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			816 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated }    #South Bucovina
		}
	}

	#We will have to deal with this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.1002.a
		trigger = {
			has_manpower > 1249
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_suppressed_resistance_in_bucovina days = 365 }
		if = {
			limit = { 80 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #North Bucovina
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			80 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #North Bucovina
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 816 = { has_state_flag = HUN_is_being_integrated } }    #South Bucovina
			add_manpower = -250
			add_political_power = -5
			816 = { custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_resistance_will_be_suppressed }    #South Bucovina
		}
	}

	#Let this run its course.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_territory.1002.b
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HUN_resistance_to_integration_in_bucovina days = 182 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_integration_in_bosnia_will_slow_down
	}
}

# Hungarian Flavor Test Events #
################################

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_test

# These events should not occur during normal gameplay

# Test event
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_test.1
	title = hungary_flavor_test.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_test.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Option 1
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_test.1.a
		every_country = {
			add_ideas = leaning_towards_germany_fascism
		}
	}

	#Option 2
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_test.1.b
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = neutrality
			size = 0.9
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = GER
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_IMP
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_tur


########
#TURKEY#
########

# [From.GetAdjective] Alliance (event for Turkey upon faction invite)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_tur.1
	title = hungary_flavor_tur.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_tur.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#This is in our best interest.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_tur.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { is_powerful_or_has_strong_friends_in_europe = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_invited_to_faction }
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.88 }
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
	}

	#A foolish proposition.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_tur.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.89 }
		}
	}
}

# Troop exchange with [From.GetName]
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_tur.2
	title = hungary_flavor_tur.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_tur.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_troop_exchange

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Their brigades will be a welcome addition to our army.
	option = {

			}

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_troop_exchange }

		add_manpower = -17990
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_tur.2.tt
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.96 } }

				limit = {
					HUN = { is_not_ahu = yes }
				}
				load_oob = exchange_HUN_to_TUR
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.97 } }

# Reawakening the Little Entente
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_yug.4
	title = hungary_flavor_yug.4.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_yug.4.d
		trigger = {
			HUN = { is_ahu = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_yug.4.d_2
		trigger = {
			HUN = { is_not_ahu = yes }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_little_entente

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We will stand against this outrage together
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_puppet = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = CZE value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = CZE value > 24 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						CZE = { has_government = neutrality }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = democratic
						CZE = { has_government = democratic }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = fascism
						CZE = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = communism
						CZE = { has_government = communism }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				AND = {
					has_government = neutrality
					CZE = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				}
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_yug.4.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = hungary_flavor_yug.4.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = { set_country_flag = little_entente_YUG_plus }
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { OR = { has_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_plus has_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_minus } } }
				CZE = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_cze.6 } }
			}
		}
	}

	#Tell them to leave us out of their petty alliance
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_flag = HUN_YUG_eternal_friendship
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_yug.4.b
		hidden_effect = {
			CZE = { set_country_flag = little_entente_YUG_minus }
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { OR = { has_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_plus has_country_flag = little_entente_ROM_minus } } }
				CZE = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor_cze.6 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

				factor = 0
				is_in_faction = yes

					NOT = { tag = GER }

				factor = 2.0
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = germany.94 } #Germany gets Slovenia
	}
	# We will stand and fight, even if alone!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_yug.9.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }

				expire = 100
					type = take_state_focus

				}
			}
		}
	}

# Hungary offers Slovenia for Burgenland
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_aus.3
	title = hungary_flavor_aus.3.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_aus.3.d_slovenia
		trigger = {
			HUN = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_austria
				NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria }
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_aus.3.d_both
		trigger = {
			HUN = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_slovenia_to_austria
				has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_aus.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { hours = 8 id = hungary_flavor.48 } }
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_country_flag = HUN_offering_ljubljana_to_austria } }
			transfer_state = 805    #Ljubljana
		}

# Imperialist coup
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_cze.2
	title = hungary_flavor_cze.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_cze.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_crowd_in_prague

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Long live the Habsburgs... I guess.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_cze.2.a

			limit = { FROM = { has_government = neutrality } }
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 0
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 100
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_government = democratic } }
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 100
				fascism = 0
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 0
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_government = fascism } }
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 100
				communism = 0
				neutrality = 0
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_government = communism } }
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 0
				fascism = 0
				communism = 100
				neutrality = 0
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_IMP
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_neighbor_of = CZE
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { hours = 6 id = hungary_flavor_gen.3 }
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor.43 } }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_imperialist_government }
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = HUN_imperialist_government }
		}
	}
}

	title = hungary_flavor_cze.9.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_cze.9.d_danub
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_danubian_coalition_member }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_cze.9.d_viseg
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_cze.9.d_faction    #This option should not trigger ever, this is only a fail-safe
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_danubian_coalition_member }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We will remember this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_cze.9.a
		HUN = {
			random_list = {
				85 = {
					transfer_state = 664 #Southern Slovakia
					add_state_core = 664 #Southern Slovakia
					if = {
						limit = { CZE = { owns_state = 802 } }    #Beregszasz
						transfer_state = 802 #Beregszasz
						add_state_core = 802 #Beregszasz
					}
				}
				15 = {}
			}
		}
	}
}

####################################
# Hungarian Flavor Election Events #
####################################

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_elections

# Election of 1939
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_elections.1
	title = hungary_flavor_elections.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_elections.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HUN
		date > 1939.1.1
		date < 1940.1.1
		has_completed_focus = HUN_dismantle_the_monarchy
	}

	#Keep the current Prime Minister
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_elections.1.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = HUN_president_kept }
	}

	#Elect Pl Teleki (NEP)
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_elections.1.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_teleki_president } }
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_hungarian_president_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = HUN_teleki_president
			create_politician_pal_teleki = yes
		}
	}

	#Elect Istvn Bethlen (NEP)
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_elections.1.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_president } }
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_hungarian_president_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = HUN_bethlen_president
			create_politician_istvan_bethlen = yes
		}
	}

	#Elect the Independent Smallholder's candidate
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_elections.1.e
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { clear_hungarian_president_flags = yes }
	}
}

add_namespace = hungary_flavor_fed_elections

# Regional elections of [ROOT.GetNameDef]
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_regional_election_flags = yes
			random_list = {
				60 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_HUN_conservatives }
				25 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_HUN_socialists }
				0 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_HUN_independence }
				15 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_HUN_liberals }
			}
			random_list = {
				45 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_AUS_conservatives }
				35 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_AUS_socialists }
				0 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_AUS_independence }
				20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_AUS_liberals }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_slovakia_is_state }
				random_list = {
					35 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_conservatives }
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_socialists }
					15 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_independence }
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_liberals }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_bohemia_moravia_is_state }
				random_list = {
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_conservatives }
					25 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_socialists }
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_independence }
					25 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_liberals }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_galicia_lodomeria_is_state }
				random_list = {
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_conservatives }
					25 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_socialists }
					35 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_independence }
					10 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_liberals }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_transylvania_is_state }
				random_list = {
					55 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_conservatives }
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_socialists }
					5 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_independence }
					10 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_liberals }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_croatia_bosnia_is_state }
				random_list = {
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_conservatives }
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_socialists }
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_independence }
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_liberals }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_carinthia_venetia_is_state }
				random_list = {
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_conservatives }
					30 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_socialists }
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_independence }
					20 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_liberals }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Let us open the ballots!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1.a
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.2 days = 7 } }
	}

	# We can not afford an election at a time like this
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1.b
		trigger = {
			surrender_progress > 0.2
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1 days = 1460 } }        #Elections again in 4 years
	}
}

# Results of the regional elections
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.2
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		print_regional_election_results = yes
	}

	# The people have spoken.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.2.a
		resolve_regional_election_results = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.1 days = 1460 }        #Elections again in 4 years
			if = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_UKR_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_YUG_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_independence }
					random_list = {
						40 = { set_country_flag = HUN_election_ITA_wants_to_break_free }
						60 = {}
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}
}

# Socialist majority in federal parliament
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.3
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.3.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		check_variable = { var = HUN_representation_socialist        value = HUN_dominance_threshold    compare = greater_than }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	# Pass the proposed social reforms.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.3.a
		step_back_economy = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -10
	}

	# Veto the reforms.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.3.b
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.10 }
	}
}

# Liberal majority in federal parliament
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.4
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.4.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		check_variable = { var = HUN_representation_liberal        value = HUN_dominance_threshold    compare = greater_than }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	# Pass the proposed liberal reforms.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.4.a
		step_back_conscription = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.10
	}

	# Veto the reforms.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.4.b
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.10 }
	}
}

# Independence parties dominate federal parliament
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.5
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.5.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		check_variable = { var = HUN_representation_independence    value = HUN_dominance_threshold    compare = greater_than }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	#Grant autonomy to the regions in question.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.5.a
		#Slovakian independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_HUN_independence }
			release_autonomous_slovakia = yes
		}

		#Bohemian independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_BOH_independence }
			release_autonomous_bohemia = yes
		}

		#Ukrainian independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_GAL_independence }
			release_autonomous_ukraine = yes
		}

		#Transylvanian independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_TRA_independence }
			release_autonomous_transylvania = yes
		}

		#Yugoslav independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_CRO_independence }
			release_autonomous_yugoslavia = yes
		}

		#Venetian and Carinthian independence/autonomy
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_election_CAR_independence }
			release_autonomous_italy = yes
			release_autonomous_slovenia = yes
		}
	}

	#Dissolve the independence parties.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.5.b
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_political_power = -300
	}
}

# Independence referendum in Slovakia pulls through
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.7
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.7.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_election_SLO_wants_to_break_free
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	# Grant them autonomy.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.7.a
		release_autonomous_slovakia = yes
	}

	# Ignore the referendum results.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.7.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

# Free of the federation (event that drops the substate cosmetic tag, if a country becomes independent after being an autonomous substate of the federation)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.12
	title = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.12.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_is_substate_of_federation
		is_subject = no
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	# We can breathe once again
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_fed_elections.12.a
		clr_country_flag = HUN_is_substate_of_federation
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
	}
}
add_namespace = hungary_flavor_gen

#########
#GENERIC#
#########


# The Danubian Coalition (Alliance with ENG and HUN for Central-Eastern European countries)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.2
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.2.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_danube

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = democratic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 9 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 19 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 19 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 29 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 29 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 39 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 19 }
			}
		}
		ENG = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "ENG"
			value = 200
		}
		set_country_flag = HUN_danubian_coalition_member
	}

	#Decline
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism }
			}
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.2.b
	}
}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_non_aggression_pact_with = HUN        #If the country has a non-aggression pact with Hungary, they shouldn't just ignore it
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_country = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_war_with = HUN        #If they are fighting against the same enemy (eg. Germany), they should prioritize that, and not jump at Hungary
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = decree_against_hungary }
			declare_war_on = { target = HUN type = puppet_wargoal_focus }
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.6 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = decree_against_hungary } }
			news_event = { hours = 4 id = hun_news.5 }
			set_country_flag = decree_against_hungary
		}
	}

	#They'll stop eventually

		name = hungary_flavor_gen.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 24 }

				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 }
			}

				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 74 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				HUN = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = decree_against_hungary
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Visegrd Group (Hungarian democratic alliance)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.5
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.5.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_visegrad_group

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					tag = CZE
					tag = POL
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				AND = {
					OR = {
						tag = LIT
						tag = LAT
						tag = EST
					}
					POL = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = democratic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 39 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 29 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 39 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 19 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 29 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 9 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 19 } }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_be_invited_into_visegrad_group
		set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}

		#Foundation is handled by an event on the Hungarian side
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CZE }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus }
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus } } }
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.100 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = POL }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus }
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus } } }
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.100 } }
			}
		}

		#Baltic expansion is handled by a different event
		if = {
			limit = { tag = LIT }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						AND = {
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus }
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.101 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = LAT }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						AND = {
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus }
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.101 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = EST }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						AND = {
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus }
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.101 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LIT
					tag = LAT
					tag = EST
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			#Baltic expansion can happen after the economic circle has already been established
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_present }
				set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_resolved
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
					reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				}
			}

		}
	}

	#Decline
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.5.b
		#Foundation is handled by an event on the Hungarian side
		if = {
			limit = { tag = CZE }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus }
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_plus } } }
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.100 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = POL }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_POL_minus }
			if = {
				limit = { HUN = { OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_CZE_plus } } }
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.100 } }
			}
		}

		#Baltic expansion is handled by a different event
		if = {
			limit = { tag = LIT }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						AND = {
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_plus }
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.101 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = LAT }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LAT_minus }
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						AND = {
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_LIT_plus }
							OR = { has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_plus }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { country_event = { hours = 4 id = hungary_flavor.101 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = EST }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_EST_minus }
			if = {

			every_country = {

				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_resolved
				every_country = {

					}

						type = alliance

					}
				}
			}

			add_to_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research
		}
	}

# Leaving the Visegrd Group (event after conventionally leaving the faction)
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.8
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.8.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HUN_visegrad_group

	is_triggered_only = yes #on_actions.txt

	#We must put this behind us.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
			clr_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle_resolved
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				has_country_flag = HUN_visegrad_group_member
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_visegrad_economic_circle }
			country_event = { days = 1 id = hungary_flavor_gen.9 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = visegrad_research
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = visegrad_military_council }
			remove_ideas = visegrad_military_council
		}
	}
}

			SOV = { transfer_state = 94 }    #Polesie
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 95 }        #Nowogrodek
			SOV = { transfer_state = 95 }    #Nowogrodek
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 96 }        #Wilejka

		}
		if = {

			SOV = { transfer_state = 97 }    #Byalistok
		}
		if = {

		}

	option = {

		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_disregarded_molotov_ribbentrop_soviet } }
	}

# Membership in the Budapest Research group
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.14
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.14.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_research_lab

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		is_in_faction_with = HUN
		HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_budapest_research_group }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_budapest_research_group_membership_offered }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_budapest_research_group_membership_offered
	}

	# Of course we will join.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = budapest_research_group
	}

# Hungary annexes Austria
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.17
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.17.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hungarian_soldiers

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_got_news_of_HUN_AUS_war }
		HUN = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_war_with_austria
			NOT = { has_war_with = AUS }
			owns_state = 4        #Lower Austria
			owns_state = 152    #Upper Austria
			owns_state = 153    #Tyrol
			owns_state = 810    #Burgenland
		}
		AUS = { exists = no }
		NOT = { tag = HUN }
		OR = {
			is_neighbor_of = HUN
			AND = {
				is_major = yes
				OR = {
					tag = ITA
					tag = GER
					tag = FRA
					tag = ENG
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_got_news_of_HUN_AUS_war
	}

	# We shall condemn this action.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				tag = ITA    #Italy supported Hungarian revisionism to some extent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_condemns_annexation_of_austria }
	}

	# Austria lies outside of our sphere of interest.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = ENG
					tag = FRA
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_government = democratic
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.19.d

		name = hungary_flavor_gen.19.a

		set_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member

			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
	}

	# On a second thought, we don't want any part of this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.19.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
}

# Joining the Danube Federation
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.20
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.20.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_communists_cheer

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_accepts_danube_federation
		has_government = communism
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = HUN }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	# Our nations are stronger together!
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		HUN = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		set_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_comittee_for_federal_security } }
			add_ideas = comittee_for_federal_security
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_federal_reserve_guard } }
			add_ideas = federal_reserve_guard
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HUN = { has_completed_focus = HUN_danube_scientific_institute } }
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = danube_scientific_institute
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "HUN"
			value = 200
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
				news_event = { id = hun_news.23 }
			}
		}
	}

	# On a second thought, we don't want any part of this.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

			remove_ideas = comittee_for_federal_security
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = federal_reserve_guard }
			remove_ideas = federal_reserve_guard
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = federal_construction_effort }
			remove_ideas = federal_construction_effort
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = danube_scientific_institute }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = danube_scientific_institute
		}
	}
}

# Our turn on the federal construction effort
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.23
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.23.t
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_gen.23.d_first
		trigger = { has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_first }
	}
	desc = {
		text = hungary_flavor_gen.23.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_first } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_done

		# If all eligible countries have already participated, the rotation starts again
		if = {
			limit = {
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member }
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member
							has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_done
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_done }
				clr_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_done
			}
		}
	}

	# We will make the most of it.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.23.a
		add_timed_idea = { idea = federal_construction_effort days = 182 }
		clr_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_first
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member
				NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_construction_effort_done }
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_be_next_target_of_effort
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor_gen.23 days = 182 } }
		}
	}
}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 74 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = UKR }
			UKR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		UKR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_returned_territory } }
	}

	# We do not wish to support such a country
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { has_government = fascism }
						has_government = democratic
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { has_government = fascism }
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_realism } }
			}
		}
		#HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.178 days = 1 } }		#FROM scope not working for some reason ([FROM.GetNameDef] shows up as an empty string)
	}
}

# Danubian workers revolt
country_event = {
	id = hungary_flavor_gen.31
	title = hungary_flavor_gen.31.t
	desc = hungary_flavor_gen.31.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot

	trigger = {
		date > 1933.1.1
		date < 1949.1.1
		has_country_flag = HUN_danubian_worker_strike
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = HUN_angered_danubian_protesters
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = HUN_danubian_worker_strike
		clr_country_flag = HUN_support_for_danubian_worker_revolution
	}

	# Accept their demands.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.31.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
			}
			release = HUN
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
			release = AUS
			AUS = { set_country_flag = HUN_liberated_by_danube_federation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
			}
			release = CZE
			CZE = { set_country_flag = HUN_liberated_by_danube_federation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
			}
			release = ROM
			ROM = { set_country_flag = HUN_liberated_by_danube_federation }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = YUG
				}
			}
			release = YUG
			YUG = { set_country_flag = HUN_liberated_by_danube_federation }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HUN_liberated_by_danube_federation
					has_country_flag = HUN_danube_federation_member
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = HUN_released_danubian_workers }
		}
		clr_country_flag = HUN_angered_danubian_protesters
		clr_country_flag = HUN_growing_danubian_protesters
		HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.183 } }
	}

	# Attempt to crush the revolt.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.31.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_angered_danubian_protesters }
			set_country_flag = HUN_will_get_danubian_worker_penalties
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_gets_fighting_bonus_danubian_workers }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_growing_danubian_protesters }
			HUN = { set_country_flag = HUN_gets_manpower_danubian_workers }
		}
		HUN = { country_event = { id = hungary_flavor.184 } }
		clr_country_flag = HUN_angered_danubian_protesters
		clr_country_flag = HUN_growing_danubian_protesters
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_will_become_responsible_for_curbing_hungarian_expansion

	# Fighting [HUN.GetName] is not in our intersts.
	option = {
		name = hungary_flavor_gen.34.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 24 }
				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 49 } }

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4

				NOT = { has_opinion = { target = HUN value > 74 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.6
